Financial Revenue and Expenditure Deficit Reaches 100 Million in Five Months in Japan

Exchange Rate Countermeasures: Conflicting Opinions in Japanese Cabinet, Shaking Political Situation; Korekiyo Takahashi Resolves to Manage Exchange Rates, Takao Nakajima Advocates Balancing Funds 50

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 10th - According to the Japanese Ministry of Finance's public announcement, in just five months from April to August of this year, the national treasury deficit has reached 126,779,000 yen. Among them, tax revenue decreased by 38,741,000 yen compared with the same period last year, stamp duty revenue decreased by 1,155,000 yen, and revenue from state-run businesses decreased by 8,860,000 yen.

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 10th - According to Finance Minister Takahashi's reply to the leaders of the Minseito Party yesterday, the Japanese Ministry of Finance intends to manage exchange rates. After ordering various banks to report the actual figures of exchange rate inflows and outflows immediately, many malpractices were discovered. Moreover, both the Seiyukai and Minseito parties will use exchange rate countermeasures as the primary issue to criticize the government. It is heard that Takahashi has made up his mind to order the Ministry of Finance to formulate various laws and regulations related to exchange rate management, which will be submitted to the 64th National Diet for review.

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 10th - Because the Japanese exchange rate continues to fall, the lives of the people are becoming increasingly difficult, especially for the middle class and officials. In view of this, both the Seiyukai and Minseito parties intend to use the exchange rate countermeasure issue to make things difficult for the government in the Diet. It is rumored that Finance Minister Takahashi will use exchange rate management as a countermeasure, ordering the Ministry of Finance to formulate a bill to be submitted to the next Diet session. Recently, Commerce Minister Nakajima suddenly opposed, saying that exchange rate management is not the best policy and that a foreign exchange equalization fund system should be adopted. The Ministry of Finance should issue five hundred million yen in treasury bonds, with the funds as collateral, so that the Bank of Japan can issue five hundred million yen in gold notes to be used for controlling exchange rates, with the loss borne by the national treasury. Nakajima said that this plan will be discussed with Railway Minister Mitsuchi and then submitted at the cabinet meeting. If so, opinions will diverge again, and obstacles to the future of the Japanese political situation will increase.

Five-Power Disarmament Talks

The German View on Equality and the French View on Security are Still Far Apart 51

National News Agency, Geneva, 9th - After a dinner party tonight, the representatives of the five major powers for disarmament talked until late at night. Although no complete agreement was reached, France is willing to allow Germany not only equality in status, but also actual equality in armaments, only insisting that Germany must gradually achieve this equality and must recognize that, according to the Treaty of Versailles, it should reduce armaments. The representatives attending the dinner party agreed to reconvene at 2:30 pm on Saturday to continue discussing this matter. Before the dinner party, British Prime Minister MacDonald had a secret talk with US representative Davis for two hours, attempting to resolve the deadlock formed by Germany's insistence on equality and France's insistence on security. Afterwards, during the dinner party, although the views of Germany and France were still far apart, they were able to eliminate some disputes. France explained in detail the reasons why its security requirements must be implemented. After discussion, the European representatives expressed the hope that the United States would guarantee non-interference when sanctions under Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant are implemented in the future, and also expressed the hope that Britain would guarantee its willingness to implement these sanctions.

Full Text of the Japanese Disarmament Proposal to be Released Today

Based on Opposition to the US Proposal, the Disarmament General Committee to Convene on Wednesday 52

Hualian News Agency, Tokyo, 10th - According to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Japanese disarmament representative formally submitted the Japanese naval disarmament proposal yesterday. This proposal was first explained to the UK, the US, Ambassador Sato to Italy and France by Ambassador Matsudaira in Geneva on the morning of the 5th, explaining Japan's true intentions. The Japanese representative said that the Japanese proposal has two major principles: first, taking defense as the principle of national defense, abolishing offensive forces; second, paying attention to the environment and special circumstances and opposing uniform reductions. The specific contents are as follows:

(1) "Battleships": The ship type, number, and armament must be reduced uniformly. (2) "Cruisers": Class A and Class B cruisers must uniformly reduce the ship type, number, and armament, just like battleships. (3) "Aircraft Carriers": These are offensive weapons, and auxiliary mother ships must be abolished together. This point is specifically aimed at the United States. (4) "Naval Aircraft": Considered offensive weapons, they must be abolished uniformly. (5) "Submarines": Submarines were the most terrifying offensive weapons during the European War. Japan believes they are defensive weapons and opposes abolishing them, only agreeing to reduce them proportionally.

Regarding Japan's proposal, diplomatic circles generally expect Japan to use avoidance of responsibility as a strategy, because opposing the proposals of the UK and the US, without proposing constructive proposals, will place the full responsibility for the failure of the meeting on Japan. This Japanese proposal, in addition to avoiding responsibility, has no new principles to be seen.

Electric Communication Agency, Tokyo, 10th - The full text of the Japanese Navy's disarmament proposal is scheduled to be released in Geneva at 7 pm today (3 am tomorrow, Japan time), and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Tokyo will also release it at the same time.

Havas News Agency, Geneva, 10th - The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference is scheduled to convene on Wednesday morning.

French Chamber of Deputies Foreign Affairs Committee Approves Repayment of US Installments

Final Attitude Still Depends on the Chamber of Deputies, Britain Decides to Settle US Debt in Cash 53

Reuters, Paris, 9th - The French Chamber of Deputies Foreign Affairs Committee today voted to approve the payment of the December installment of the debt owed to the US, but this resolution is conditional on convening a general assembly to investigate the war debt issue. French Prime Minister Herriot reported on recent events before the Foreign Affairs Committee vote, especially on talks related to financial and diplomatic events. The French Prime Minister has now received a reply from the United States, which rejects the deferral of the December debt installment and reiterates President Hoover's view that the war debt issue can be resolved in the future by commercially compensating the United States. The US reply to France is generally the same as the letter to Britain, acknowledging that the French government, like other governments, faces significant difficulties in the budget, but stating that the current payment and its remittance do not seem to have a significant adverse impact on the world economy or the recovery of prosperity. President Hoover acknowledged the value of France's explanation of the flow of cash into France, but said that France's possession of this gold seems to be closely related to the current difficulty in remittance. It is expected that the French Prime Minister will not change his policy of paying the December installment. As for whether France should break its promise, thus destroying the Anglo-French agreement within the week, it is up to the Chamber of Deputies to decide.

Reuters, London, 9th - It is heard that the British government has decided to settle the US debt installment due on December 15 in cash, totaling US$95.5 million. This cash may be transferred through accounts, so it may not be shipped to the United States immediately.

German Parliament Adjourns

Government's Future Full of Thorns 54

National News Agency, Berlin, 9th - The German Parliament adjourned today, with no date set for reconvening. It is expected to reopen around January 15. Before the adjournment today, a bill was passed, revoking part of the emergency decree issued by President Hindenburg in September, which allowed employers to reduce wages after hiring additional workers, declaring that Parliament does not recognize wage cuts as a necessary part of economic reform. Also, a pardon bill was passed by a vote of 595 to 144, either releasing or greatly reducing the sentences of all political prisoners, and stipulating that criminal offenses arising from economic decline should be reduced in punishment. However, there were no changes regarding capital punishment and penalties for violating the ban on political terrorism, and penalties for treason and violation of regulations on storing explosive materials.

National News Agency, Berlin, 10th - Most newspapers regard the adjournment of Parliament as a victory for Chancellor Schleicher, because Schleicher can take a breather during the adjournment period to prepare his administrative procedures and be able to silence the opposition party when Parliament reconvenes in January next year. However, Schleicher's future still has many thorns, because the Nazi Party may not support him again in the future. Newspapers expect that Parliament may be dissolved again in January next year.

Internal Strife Within the German Nazi Party 55

Reuters, Berlin, 10th - There is a growing trend of disobedience to Hitler's leadership within the Nazi Party, due to dissatisfaction with Hitler's policy of not getting everything and getting nothing. The leader of the opposition is Strasser, who is the director of the National Organization Department of the Nazi Party. Although he opposes Hitler now, he has not yet openly rebelled against him. Strasser is currently on a three-week leave of absence. Some say that this diplomatic leave is the beginning of a major split in the Nazi Party. Strasser advocates showing some leniency towards the Schleicher government to avoid the possibility of a new election, but Hitler firmly rejects this proposal. Shortly after the announcement of Strasser's three-week leave of absence, Strasser's close friend Feder, the director of the economic division of the Nazi Party, was also reported to be on leave. It is heard that Feder wrote to Hitler, claiming that the current policy adopted by the party hinders the party's power, and that the government's economic department should not be dissolved to avoid causing misunderstandings and losing trust. It is heard that Nazi welfare official Frick and influential journalist Rosenberg are also among the opposition. It is rumored that the opposition has gained the sympathy of at least 50 of the 195 Nazi members of parliament. According to the views of Strasser and others, Hitler's desire to be elected to the presidency prevents the Nazi Party's movement from being combined with the application of national construction power. After Strasser and others took leave, the radicals in the party, such as Parliament Speaker Goering, became more powerful.

US Government Reduction Plan

Massive Merger of Redundant Agencies, Changes in the Functions of Various Departments and Bureaus 57

National News Agency, Washington, 9th - The US President's reform plan to massively merge redundant agencies and change the functions of various departments and bureaus has been made into a special report, which was released in Congress this afternoon. The content includes the abolition of several larger bureaus and committees, and the merger and reorganization of 58 offices. Four deputy ministers are added to the Department of the Interior, responsible for education, public works, health and fitness, and agriculture and land use. All redundant agencies related to these categories are merged into the department, that is, most of the engineering duties currently under the Army Department, including important river and harbor projects, will be transferred to the Department of the Interior. Also, all merchant ship agencies, such as the Shipping Bureau and the Emergency Fleet Corporation, are merged into the Department of Commerce. As for the program to save government expenses after the merger, the President's report did not estimate it, only stating that the expenses of the agencies currently being merged total 700 million gold yuan per year, and a large portion should be saved after the merger is implemented. Also, if Congress does not object to this reform plan, it will be implemented in two months.

British Industrial Leaders Advocate Boycotting Dumping of Japanese Goods

Three Measures Decided, Japanese Goods Will Have No Foothold in the British Empire 59

Reuters, London, 10th - A meeting was held in Manchester today and resolved to hold a citizens' meeting in the entire city of Lancashire to oppose foreign cotton fabrics competing with British goods, especially Japanese textiles, being dumped in Indian British colonies and territories. The attendees of today's meeting were mostly leading cotton spinners, manufacturers, merchants, and shippers. A resolution was passed requesting the government to find ways to curb competition, and three measures were proposed as follows: (1) British goods in Indian colonies and territories should not be subject to import duties except for national taxes. (2) The taxes levied in the above areas should give British products a fair opportunity to compete. (3) The above plan should be in line with appropriate agreements on preferential trade between various parts of the British Empire.

German Professor to Lecture in China 60

National News Agency, Berlin, 9th - German newspapers expressed great satisfaction with the Chinese government's invitation to German scientist Professor Muller to come to China to lecture and continue research work. Muller is the director of the Hamburg Institute of Tropical Diseases and a mathematician known worldwide. His stay in China will be about five months and will lecture at universities in Guangzhou, Shanghai, Beiping, Hong Kong, and other places in China.

US Farmers Petition Congress 61

National News Agency, Washington, 9th - Today, US farmers went to Congress to petition, gathering in the audience seats, and striving to have their petitions accepted first, and then discussing other cases. Even the President's special report on reorganizing government agencies was regarded as insignificant. Congress had no choice but to read their petitions first, and the reading of the President's report was delayed for two hours. The content of their petitions focused on rescuing agriculture, demanding the enactment of laws sufficient to raise prices, and suspending payments on rural loans, and listing many previously petitioned relief plans. After the reading of the petitions was completed, the farmers left together, and Congress was able to read the President's report. It is reported that several committees in Congress have already begun to consider rural relief plans, but although this move is the most urgent plan at present, it is very difficult to handle. The plan to increase tariffs proposed by the Republican Party may be abandoned because the Democratic government will oppose increasing tariffs.

The Great Success of the Fascist Exhibition (Rome Communication)

— Jingfu

The Pride in the Success and Spirit of the Italian Fascists Ten Years Ago 62

Italy participated in the European War as one of the Allied powers, and its sacrifices were second only to France. Therefore, although it possessed the name of a victorious country after the war, its vitality was declining and people's livelihood was deteriorating, and it was almost unable to recover. Coupled with the rampant red forces, all industries were abandoned, and the domestic economy was even more desolate, to the point where it could not be salvaged. Mussolini took the opportunity to rise up, establish the Fascist regime, save the situation from collapse, and enable Italy to return to strength. Mussolini's great achievements are truly indelible events in history, and they were also created by the opportunity. Ten years ago, in June 1922, after the Fascists destroyed the Socialist Party's General Alliance strike plan and then went on to destroy its base camp, Mussolini's momentum was unstoppable. At that time, the Italian government was the weak and incompetent Facta cabinet, so the domestic industrialists and businessmen had already hoped that Mussolini would come out and take power at this time. Unfortunately, the Fascists were an absolute minority in parliament, and it was impossible to gain power through peaceful means, so they had to resort to violence and decided to launch an attack on October 28, occupying important cities and marching on Rome. In two days, the overall situation was settled, and the Fascist regime was established. It has been exactly ten years until the end of October this year, so it was decided to hold a grand celebration to celebrate the success of the Fascists.

The National Beiping Library Newly Collects a Large Batch of Antiques

The Ho Family of Houguan Deposits Them, and a Special Room Will Be Opened for Display 63

Since the establishment of the new National Beiping Library, many collectors at home and abroad have deposited rare books and antiques. After the Liang family of Xinhui deposited their family collection of books and inscriptions in the library, others followed suit every year, such as Zhu Min of Zijiang depositing the legacy of the German Mullendorf, and Qu of Changsha depositing his family collection of books. He Sui (号叙甫) of Houguan is famous for collecting Han tile ends. This spring, he deposited a part of the tile ends, as well as a tombstone of the great chieftain of the United States from the Tang Kaiyuan period of the New Germany, a vermilion-written Xiping four-year tile pot, and a vermilion-written Heng character tile. In the autumn and winter, Ho returned from his tour of Shaanxi and deposited all the antiques he had obtained over the years in the library for safekeeping. There are 660 Han and Tang tile ends, 130 Han and Tang ancient mirrors, including an iron mirror inlaid with mother-of-pearl, which is the rarest item, as well as 125 Yin Ruins oracle bones, a full copy of the original rubbings of ancient New Zheng artifacts, two large boxes and eight thick volumes of other bronze and stone rubbings, and 20 volumes of Chen Zhongzhai's collection of tile end rubbings, including a volume of tile end rubbings from Lelang Prefecture, which is the most precious, as well as 24 volumes of Ho's family collection of tile end rubbings, a Han Miao bronze drum, a Han foundation stone glazed head, four Qin and Han mausoleum bricks, a stone carving of the Heart Sutra in Tang Fei Xiu's calligraphy, a rubbing of the iron pagoda in the sixth year of the Southern Han Dabaobao, the pagoda is in Guangzhou, 18 feet high, and some other scattered small items, as well as books, painting albums, and photos. It is heard that the library intends to open a special room for display to encourage those who are inspired by the news.

Although the grand anniversary celebration of this year is scheduled for October 28, it has actually been celebrated throughout the country since October 1, so it is no exaggeration to call October the celebration month. Among the various arrangements for the celebration, the most noteworthy is the exhibition of achievements over the past ten years. Among them, the two exhibitions, "Victory of the Grain War" and "Development of New Cultivated Land," are the most interesting, because Mussolini regarded these as his greatest achievements, so he specifically listed them in detail, but the general audience found them too numerous. The entrance to the halls where the exhibits are displayed is decorated with huge words "Faith, Obedience, Struggle," which are the supreme beliefs of the Fascists and are truly representative of the spirit of their general members. In the "Exhibition of Revolutionary Deeds" Hall in Via Naziona, four huge axes are displayed to symbolize the Fascists' destruction of all old forces. All the relics of the internal strife in Italy from 1919 to 1922 are listed here. There are more than 17,000 pieces of collected historical materials, but the "victims of internal strife" enshrined in them are limited to Fascist Party members. The collection of historical materials begins with Mussolini's advocacy of joining the Allied forces to participate in the war. The first issue of Mussolini's Italian People's Daily, which he founded, was enlarged to a huge size and displayed,

First (the publication date of the first issue was November 15, 1914), seeing it still makes people imagine Mussolini in the Milan editorial office at that time. According to the order of display, going on to view the various exhibition halls, the Fascists' movement starting from Milan, the twists and turns, the recoveries, and the final seizure of power to the success of today are all displayed without omission according to their historical progress. The layout is actually a large-scale historical museum, but its vibrant spirit is incomparable to ordinary museums.

Being in it is like personally participating in the struggle of the past eighteen years. Another section is dedicated to displaying various domestic and foreign works on Mussolini's life and the Fascists, totaling more than 3,000 kinds, in various languages. Mussolini's portraits and sculptures are everywhere, totaling no less than several thousand kinds, large and small. Mussolini's slogans and maxims are used in huge characters and in various colors to reflect on the halls, and the handwriting of the famous Italian writer D'Annunzio is also displayed to accompany them. The furnishings and decorations of the exhibition hall are not very gorgeous, because they do not want to hinder the expression of the revolutionary spirit due to the decorations, but the art of the Futurists can be seen everywhere, and the heroic spirit that fills all the arrangements is especially the characteristic felt by the viewers. "Italy is ours! Italy is ours!" "Three days of Fascism is better than four years of incompetent government!" This is indeed the proud words of the Fascists, and their achievements are also worthy of pride. This exhibition in Rome fully expresses this spirit. (Posted on November 6)

The Suppression of Bandits Headquarters Organizes Party Affairs in Three Provinces 64

(County Party Headquarters to have Cadres and Assistants, all Unpaid; Party Fees and Member Donations No Longer Provided by the Government; Party Departmental Titles, Seals, and Documents Must Eliminate Officialdom)

Hankou Correspondence: The Headquarters for the Suppression of Bandits in the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui recently formulated the "Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui." After submission to the 48th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee, it was approved for record. On the 9th, the Headquarters officially announced the full text of the outline by order and sent separate letters to the Provincial and Municipal Party Headquarters for implementation. The outline contains many reforms regarding the organization of lower-level Party Headquarters. Excerpts of the order and outline are recorded below:

(Order) "Order One": The Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has now been formulated and submitted to the 48th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee. It is hereby approved for record and officially promulgated. This order. "Order Two": Notification Regarding the Formulation of the Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, submitted to the 48th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee and approved for record, has been publicly announced by the Headquarters. In addition to sending separate letters to the Provincial Party Headquarters of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, as well as the Hankou Municipal Party Headquarters, to implement the outline and instruct all subordinate Party Headquarters to comply accordingly, we hereby copy and issue the Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui for your information and instruction to your subordinates. This order. "Letter to the Party Headquarters of the Three Provinces and the Hankou Special Municipality": In response to the fact that the Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui has been formulated and submitted to the 48th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee, it has been approved for record and publicly announced by the Headquarters. In addition to sending separate letters and notifications, we hereby send a copy of the Provisional Outline for the Reorganization of Party Affairs in the Bandit Suppression Zone of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui to your Party Headquarters for implementation in accordance with the provisions of the outline and instruct all subordinate County and District Party Headquarters to comply accordingly. Please report the implementation status.

(Outline) 1. Party affairs in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui shall be reorganized in accordance with this outline. 2. Except for the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Special Municipal Party Headquarters of the three provinces, which shall continue to operate in accordance with the current regulations, the County Party Headquarters shall be temporarily reorganized to have one cadre and one assistant cadre, who shall be fully responsible for reorganizing Party affairs in their respective counties. However, counties with fewer than 200 Party members shall jointly establish a Party Headquarters with two or more counties. 3. Cadres and assistant cadres shall be selected from loyal and capable comrades who currently hold positions in the local area or have stable occupations and whose livelihoods do not depend on Party sustenance. 4. The selection of cadres and assistant cadres shall be conducted by the Provincial Party Headquarters in accordance with the County Party Headquarters Cadre Selection Rules formulated by the Headquarters, selecting qualified personnel and submitting a list to the Headquarters for approval. 5. Cadres and assistant cadres of each county shall be periodically rotated and trained by the Provincial Party Headquarters in accordance with the County Party Headquarters Cadre Training Rules formulated by the Headquarters. 6. Cadres and assistant cadres shall be unpaid. The necessary expenses of the Party Headquarters shall be kept to a minimum and shall be covered by donations from Party members in the respective counties. They shall not be provided by the Provincial or County Treasury or diverted from local public funds, in order to set an example of Party members supporting the Party. 7. County Party Headquarters cadres, together with assistant cadres, shall, in addition to handling the usual affairs of their respective Party Headquarters, earnestly carry out the following matters: 1. Propagating Party doctrine; 2. Improving Party affairs; 3. Training Party members; 4. Strictly enforcing Party discipline; 5. Party members should set their own rules and encourage each other to cultivate the Party's virtues of diligence, courage, trustworthiness, and loyalty; 6. Paying attention to discovering outstanding individuals with good character and talent in various localities and introducing them to the Party to strengthen the Party's foundation. 8. The titles, seals, and document formats of Party departments shall be separately prescribed. They shall not hang plaques similar to those of government offices, or use seals similar to those of government offices, or continue to use the document formats and styles of government offices, in order to correct the bad habits of Party officialdom and Party officials. Except for the mutual relations between Party Headquarters or between Party Headquarters and Party members, the Party Headquarters or Party members shall not act externally in the name of the Party Headquarters or Party members, and in particular, they shall not interfere in local administrative or judicial affairs in the name of the Party Headquarters or Party members. However, if government officials are found to have engaged in illegal or derelict conduct, the County Party Headquarters may collect factual evidence and report it to the Provincial Party Headquarters for transmission to the Headquarters or the Provincial Government for investigation and prosecution. 9. If Party members serve in government agencies at all levels or local organizations and participate in various professional groups, and can effectively promote Party doctrine, temper Party virtues, and win the faith of the public, thereby leading to the daily development of Party affairs, the superior Party Headquarters shall investigate and commend them accordingly. Those who violate Party regulations, violate Party discipline, and engage in self-interest or self-degradation in the name of the Party shall be reported to the superior Party Headquarters at any time and given warnings or expulsion. Rewards and punishments must be given separately every six months. 10. The expenses of the Provincial Party Headquarters and the Special Municipal Party Headquarters shall be quickly planned to be self-sufficient, and after the 22nd year, they shall no longer be provided by the Provincial Treasury. 11. Matters not covered in this outline may be handled with reference to the principles and implementation plan for improving the organization and activities of Party Headquarters below the county and city levels, and general existing Party regulations and laws, as adopted by the 26th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Executive Committee. 12. This outline shall be implemented after being submitted to the Central Executive Committee for approval and record. (December 9th)

He Chengjun Returns to Hankou

Northern Hubei Administrative Office Revoked; Fan and Zhang Share Defense Responsibilities 65

Hankou Correspondence: He Chengjun, Pacification Commissioner stationed in Hubei, previously received an order from Chairman Chiang to be stationed in Laohekou to supervise the suppression of Xu and He's remnant bandits. An office was established there, and he personally assumed command. Subsequently, due to the intrusion of Red Bandits deep into Shaanxi Province, Shaanxi Chairman Yang Hucheng telegraphed requesting that he move to Xi'an to supervise the suppression from nearby. He Chengjun agreed to go immediately, but due to a sudden onset of hemorrhoids, requiring urgent treatment, he was unable to make the trip. Instead, he dispatched Chen Guangzu, Director of the Pacification Office, as his representative to report on everything. At this time, Chairman Chiang telegraphed summoning him to Hankou for a face-to-face inquiry about the bandit suppression situation. He Chengjun originally intended to return south by plane, but due to his illness, he was unable to fly. Therefore, he returned to Hankou by car on the morning of the 8th. The day before, he convened Northern Hubei generals in Laohekou and gave instructions on post-bandit suppression and post-disaster relief. He also telegraphed the troops pursuing the bandits into Shaanxi Province to actively suppress the remnant bandits and personally went to various hospitals to comfort the wounded and sick officers and soldiers involved in the bandit suppression, distributing funds for recuperation, amounting to 200 yuan per person for colonels and regimental commanders, 100 yuan per person for majors and battalion commanders, 50 yuan per person for captains and company commanders, 30 yuan for lieutenants, 20 yuan for second lieutenants, 10 yuan for warrant officers, 6 yuan per person for seriously wounded soldiers, 1 yuan per person for sick soldiers, and 5 yuan per person for sick officers. At 7:00 AM on the 8th, accompanied by all personnel of the Administrative Office, Chief of Staff Guan Linshu, Senior Staff Officer Yang Yadong, Councilor Xiong Zhiyuan, Staff Officers Xu Xuzhong and Guan Wenhui, Secretary Li Peng, Aides-de-Camp Wen Zhenfan and Zhao Yixue, and Quartermaster Zhu Xiangwen, etc., he departed Laohekou in seventeen cars, and the Administrative Office was immediately revoked. At 9:30 AM, he arrived in Fancheng, passed through Zaoyang County at around 10:00 AM, and arrived in Huayuan at 6:00 PM. At 12:00 PM that evening, he boarded a special train on the Pinghan Railway to the south, without stopping along the way. At 3:00 AM on the 9th, he arrived at the Dazhimen Station in Hankou, where various dignitaries welcomed him. After getting off the train, he returned to his private residence to rest, as the sky was still dark. At 8:00 AM, he went to Yihua Village to meet with Chairman Chiang and report on the bandit suppression and the latest deployments. At 1:00 PM, he went to the Pacification Office to review documents and meet with Zhu Shaoliang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Border Area of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, Li Dingwu, Commander of the Third Brigade, Chen Han, Director of the Tenth Army's Hankou Office, and Wang Shiliu and Yu Yuzhi, members of the Provincial Party Headquarters. In the evening, he made the following statement to the press: 1. When the two groups of Red Bandits, Xu Xiangqian and He Long, previously fled to Northern Hubei, they led more than 16,000 bandits. After our army's successive encirclements and suppressions, more than half of them were lost. Currently, Xu's bandits only have 4,000 to 5,000 people left, and He's bandits only have 1,000 to 2,000 people left, fleeing to Foping, west of Xi'an and south of Fengxiang. When the remnant bandits entered Shaanxi, Shaanxi Chairman Yang Hucheng telegraphed requesting that I go to Xi'an to command and supervise the suppression. Commander-in-Chief Chiang also telegraphed urging me to go, but due to my hemorrhoids not healing, I was unable to make the trip. Currently, the military affairs of bandit suppression have been entrusted to Shaanxi Army's Feng Qincai Division, and Zhang Hongyuan and Wang Zhiyuan's brigades, together with the pursuit units, are encircling and suppressing them. Before I arrive in Xi'an, the command will be temporarily under Director Yang Hucheng. Chen Zhixin (i.e., Chen Guangzu) was previously dispatched to Shaanxi to consult with Yang. He departed from Xi'an on the 8th and spent the night in Tongguan, returning to Hankou via Zhengzhou on the 9th. There are still many scattered bandits hiding in Northern Hubei, so troops must be stationed there to defend it. The area west of Laohekou has been assigned to Fan Shisheng's 51st Division to clear and suppress, and the Xiangfan area has been assigned to Zhang Zhenhan's 41st Division to clear and suppress. The deployments are now in place. After the disaster in Northern Hubei, the markets are deserted. Local self-defense and baojia have been started, but it remains to be seen how complete and proper they will be. 2. The Sichuan Army is returning to Sichuan, and Yichang will be taken over by the 9th Division. The handover is imminent. Because of the heavy task of suppressing bandits, I originally planned not to attend the Third Plenary Session, so I did not prepare any proposals. Recently, I received telegraphic requests from various parties, so I decided to attend. I will leave Hankou for Nanjing in the coming days." (December 9th)

Garrison Troop Adjustments in Southern Jiangxi and Guangdong-Guangxi 66

(First Army Reinforces with a Brigade to Station in Shangyou; Zhang Division of the Second Army Transfers to Xinfeng Area; Wang Division of the Guangxi Army Takes Over San'nan in Xinfeng)

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since the Liu Zhennian's troops have been stationed in northern Fujian, the strength of the bandit suppression army in Jiangxi Province has greatly increased. The communist bandits led by Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Dong Zhentang, and Luo Binghui, who had gathered on the border of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, and Fujian, now have a plan to flee again. Therefore, there are widespread rumors that the Jiangxi communist bandits have a tendency to attack Zhejiang and flee to Guangdong. However, based on their actual strength, the pseudo-Fifth Army Group is scattered in the northwest of Fujian Province, and Peng Dehuai's pseudo-Third Army Group is eyeing Nancheng and Nanfeng. In addition to the central army units of Jiangxi Province encircling the bandit area, the central government has again dispatched two divisions to Jiangxi to assist in the suppression, aiming to wipe them out in one fell swoop. In Fujian Province, the supplementary brigade of Tan Qixiu was recently dispatched to Yongchun on the 28th of last month. Commander Tan has already led the third regiment of Zheng Xingcha, the guard regiment of Li Jinbo, to their destination to search for the remnants of Chen Guohui and guard against the disturbances of the local communists. As for the southern Jiangxi area, in order to strictly prevent the communist bandits from fleeing south, the Guangdong army has also been actively deploying, with various units transferring to consolidate defenses. The southwest of Jiangxi is still being guarded by Yu Hanmou's First Army. Recently, in order to increase strength, Commander Yu has telegraphed the Second Independent Brigade of Chen Zhang in the rear to go to Shangyou for joint defense. After receiving the order, Chen Zhang is scheduled to depart from Dayu on the 6th. The terrain in the San'nan and Xinfeng areas is also important. A few days ago, 2,000 communist bandits attacked Xinfeng City from Wangmu Ferry. The Guangxi Army's Wang Zanbin Division counterattacked, and Zhang Meixin's Fourth Division of the Guangdong Army in San'nan also attacked from Longnan. Last month, they successfully defeated the Wangmu Ferry communist bandits and captured a large number of them. After this battle, the Guangdong and Guangxi armies in the area believed that it was necessary to change the joint defense, so they agreed to transfer the Fourth Division of the Second Army in San'nan with Wang Zanbin's Guangxi Army in Xinfeng. After receiving the order, the two division commanders Wang Zanbin's Division telegraphed the Shaoguan rear office to send the healed wounded soldiers to Xinfeng for replenishment in order to move with the team. It is reported that the two divisions of Zhang and Wang began to move on the 1st of this month. The 44th Division of the Guangxi Army, Wang Zanbin's troops, stationed in Xinfeng, marched to San'nan, and the defense of Xinfeng was taken over by Zhang Meixin's Fourth Division of the Guangdong Army. The Second Army's headquarters also moved to Xinfeng with the Fourth Division, with Zhang Meixin still serving as the director of the Second Army's headquarters. The Fourth Division's 10th Regiment of Wu Jianxiong, the 11th Regiment of Kong Kequan, and the 12th Regiment of Chen Jing had already moved into the territory of Xinfeng from the defense of San'nan since the 2nd. The Teaching Regiment of Jiang Wu also returned to Xinfeng City from the vicinity of Anyuan. As soon as the deployment is completed, Zhang Meixin will return to the province to report everything and ask for instructions on future strategies. (December 5th)

Increased Import Tax in the Nanyang Islands

Decision to Implement on New Year's Day; Great Impact on the Sales of National Goods 67

Shantou Correspondence: The British Nanyang Malay Islands have always adopted an open trade free system, roughly the same as Hong Kong. However, in recent years, the world's economic situation has undergone major changes, and industries have declined. The Nanyang's local products, such as rubber and tin ingots, have been greatly affected. Therefore, the number of unemployed Chinese workers in the Malay Islands has increased sharply. The local government and overseas Chinese charitable organizations have immediately set up methods to accommodate the unemployed overseas Chinese and subsidize their return home. The British government has also issued orders to restrict the entry of Chinese workers, stipulating the number of passengers carried by ships from Shantou, Xiamen, Hong Kong, and Haikou each month. Each ship should sell tickets in proportion to the average number of passengers carried on weekdays. This regulation was promulgated in the spring of the previous year. Due to the ever-deteriorating economic situation in Nanyang, the regulation has been extended repeatedly, and the number of Chinese immigrants has gradually decreased. At present, the British Straits Settlements government only allows Shantou, Hong Kong, Xiamen, and Haikou to allow 900 Chinese to enter each month, which is independently controlled by the Da Xin, Da Gu, and He Tong shipping companies. However, these 900 people are cabin passengers, and women, children, and second-class cabin passengers holding passports are not restricted. In the past, about 10,000 overseas Chinese from Shantou went to Nanyang every month, but now the four ports combined are less than a thousand. Those seeking a living abroad naturally feel a sense of despair, but the shipping companies also suffer the same pain, because the expenses of each ship cannot be arbitrarily reduced due to this. Moreover, the relationship between Shantou and Singapore, the cargo transportation business, is also quite profitable. Therefore, the shipping companies, on the one hand, transfer their ships to routes to Siam, Saigon, Rangoon, Luzon, the Yangtze River, and the Chinese coast, and on the other hand, increase passenger fares. The price of a cabin ticket to Singapore was 36 yuan per ticket two years ago, then increased to 56 yuan, and now it has increased to 90 yuan. This is the official price of the agency company. Due to the fact that demand exceeds supply, each ticket often sells for more than 100 yuan. It is difficult for ordinary people to buy it unless they have a familiar inn to buy it for them. Furthermore, according to returning visitors from Singapore, the Legislative Council of the British Straits Settlements government has passed a regulation to increase import tariffs on goods, which will be implemented from New Year's Day next year. This move is of great concern to Chinese business, because since the September 18th Incident, overseas Chinese have been happy to use national goods. The new products manufactured in Shanghai, such as porcelain, ironware, and canned food from Chaoshan, have a large market in the Nanyang Islands via Singapore. If tariffs are increased, the emerging vitality of Chinese goods will be greatly frustrated. Local Chinese merchants are certainly opposed to this, and Chaoshan merchants are also very concerned about it. (December 2nd)

Jiangsu and Shandong Will Jointly Manage Transportation

Shandong Construction Department Sends Personnel to Attend the Huai River Guidance Committee 68

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Construction Department has been actively preparing this year to dredge the southern Shandong Canal to promote water conservancy. The canal's tributaries, such as the Niutou River, the east and west Si Rivers, etc., will be completed one after another. Next spring, the canal itself will be dredged. Jiangsu opposed Shandong's independent management of transportation, and the dispute has not been resolved for a long time. Recently, the Huai River Guidance Committee held a meeting in Nanjing and sent a letter inviting Shandong Province to send personnel to participate. The dispute over the management of transportation between Jiangsu and Shandong will be discussed, with the aim of joint implementation. Zhang Honglie, Director of the Construction Department, has now dispatched technician Shi Andong and Kong Lingrong, Director of the Canal Engineering Bureau, to attend. Shi and Kong are scheduled to depart from Jinan on the 9th. I once visited Cao Liqing, Chief of the Construction Department, to inquire about everything. According to Cao, the rivers in southern Shandong have not been dredged for a long time. The Weishan Lake stores too much water, while the canal releases too little, losing its regulatory function. Most tributaries such as the Si River flow into Weishan Lake, averaging 1,000 cubic meters of water per second, while the canal only releases 400 to 500 cubic meters per second. If this continues, a large amount of rain in autumn and summer will cause floods, which is dangerous. Therefore, dredging the canal in this province is a crucial plan. The Jiangsu side is currently preparing to build the Lanjia Dam in Tongshan County and widen the Bulao River to divert the flow. The representatives of Shandong attending the Huai River Guidance Committee intend to request that Jiangsu limit the height of the Lanjia Dam in order to avoid obstructing the flow of water. If Jiangsu and Shandong can jointly dredge, so that the canal discharges more than 400 cubic meters per second, the Bulao River discharges 500 cubic meters per second, and the Yin River in Yixian County, Shandong, also discharges 170 cubic meters per second, then floods can be eliminated, and both provinces will benefit. (December 8th)

Songjiang

Big Cake Shop Owner Commits Assault While Shopping 69

Huang Lisan, an Anhui native, has been running a big cake shop on the Qianjie of the county for many years. The shop owner is extremely irritable and often quarrels with people. Today (the 10th) at 9:00 AM, a peddler named Wang Yinqiu came to the big cake shop to trade, carrying sweet potatoes on his shoulder for sale. Due to a dispute over the price, the shop owner immediately raised the knife for cutting cakes and stabbed the peddler Wang Yinqiu several times in the head and shoulder, causing blood to flow all over the ground. Passersby, filled with indignation, immediately called the police to arrest the assailant Huang Lisan and sent him and the injured Wang Yinqiu to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. It is now reported that Wang was sent to Songjiang County Hospital for treatment and is not in imminent danger, but his injuries are quite serious.

Financial Bureau Conceals Funds for Provincial Education, Detained and Pursued 70

Xiao Zenrong, the former director of the Financial Bureau, served for more than a year. The bureau affairs were always presided over by Section Chief Feng Gengbai. He arbitrarily concealed and did not report the number of education funds that should be remitted to the Provincial Education Foundation and deposited them in the name of the Public Account at Songjiang Bank, hoping to earn interest. Later, the bank went bankrupt. The Provincial Education Management Office considered the situation to be corrupt and inferior, and requested the Provincial Government to order the Finance Department to immediately remove and detain him for investigation. The Finance Department ordered the county to investigate and reply. Last month, Xiao died of illness in Hangzhou and was temporarily replaced by Section Chief Feng. Now, Shen Bingde, a provincial commissioner, came to Songjiang to take office. Yesterday, during the liquidation and handover, Yang Zixian, Section Chief of the Foundation Office, and Sun Guozhang, a commissioner, came to Songjiang and found out that Xiao owed more than 23,000 yuan in education funds that should be remitted to the province, and that more than 53,000 yuan had been concealed, totaling more than 76,000 yuan. Only 15,000 yuan was remitted at the beginning of this month. They immediately telegraphed Director Niu Yongjian for instructions. Niu telegraphed County Magistrate Shen to strictly detain and pursue the personnel handled by Xiao until the full amount is recovered before they are released.

Disputes Arise Over Inspection of New Scales 71

Yesterday morning, when the Yue Temple vegetable market was busy with transactions, Shi, an inspector from the County Bureau of Weights and Measures, came to inspect. He found that the scales held by general buyers had not been corrected and collected them one by one, numbering more than 40. Subsequently, a certain cook protested, arguing that the peddlers had not yet corrected the scales according to the new regulations, so why should the buyers be asked to correct them first, causing obstacles to the transaction? Moreover, the value of a scale is at least more than one yuan, and the poor cannot afford to buy it. Moreover, the method of calculating new and old has not been fully publicized, and it is reckless to carry out suppression, which is close to punishing without teaching. The inspector immediately called the police to detain the cook and sent him to the Second Precinct. For a time, vegetable farmers gathered and almost caused a disturbance. After the supervisors of the Public Security Bureau persuaded them on the spot, the crowd gradually dispersed.

Qingpu

Three-Year-Old Child Suddenly Kidnapped by Bandits 72

On the night of the 7th, more than ten bandits speaking with a northern accent suddenly came to the Luo Heqing home in Zhujiacun Township, Second District. One person pulled out a handgun to prohibit any noise, and the remaining bandits kidnapped Zhu's three-year-old son and left. There is still no news to this day, and the family is very anxious and is now trying to rescue him.

Agricultural Education Hall Organizes Cooperative 73

The Qingpu Agricultural Education Hall, in view of the extreme decline of the rural economy in recent years, unless methods are found to provide relief as soon as possible, it will inevitably fall into distress, so today (the 8th) it convened nearby villagers to initiate the organization of a credit purchase cooperative. It is now in the process of proceeding, and it can be scheduled to be established as soon as the procedures are complete.

Suzhou

After the Robbery of the Yutai Steamer 74

The Yutai steamer traveling to Dongting East Mountain in Suzhou was robbed at 3:30 PM on the 9th. While passing through the Wangxiao Bay area, it encountered bandits robbing passengers Jin Youbo, Yan, etc. Four officers of the Water Police 8th Team, escorting the steamer, were shot and killed in a firefight, three were injured, and stray bullets hit two passengers. The bandits fled to West Taihu Lake. The situation has been reported in this newspaper. After the incident, the Water Police 3rd District, the county police, and the Suzhou-Songjiang water bandit suppression department all dispatched teams to pursue the bandits on the same day, but the bandits had gone far and could not be captured. Now, Shen, the head of the 3rd District of the Water Police, believes that in order to comfort and defend the Water Police 8th Team of Dongshan, which has gone to Taihu Lake to pursue the bandits, he has mobilized the police team to dispatch the 3rd Brigade to Dongshan to thicken security. Due to the robbery of the patrol ship's guns, which is like giving wings to a tiger, the Wuxian County Chamber of Commerce believes that the Wangxiao Bay area is a vital route of travel and that the bandits are rampant and terrifying to merchants. It is necessary to establish a stronghold in the area to house a patrolling force. On the 10th, they sent a telegram to the Civil Affairs Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Government requesting that it swiftly be ordered to encircle and suppress the bandits, to recover the kidnapped travelers, to maintain safe travel, and to uphold commerce.

Garrison Police and Gendarmes Connect to Protect the Road 75

In order to maintain the security of the Jinghu (Nanjing-Shanghai) Railway, the Capital Gendarmerie Headquarters stipulated that police from each county and security corps should strengthen their liaison with the railway gendarmes in order to ensure maximum security. On the 10th, Tang Jiaju was dispatched to Suzhou to meet with County Magistrate Zou at the county government to discuss the rail line protection between Weiting and Wangting.

Fengxian

Resolution of the Fengnan Boundary Issue 76

After several consultations between representatives of the two counties on the Fengnan boundary issue, the two sides' opinions gradually approached. Therefore, yesterday (the 9th), the governments of the two counties of Fengnan held a joint meeting in Shen's Lotus Garden in Nanqiao. The attendees included Kong Chong, County Magistrate of Nanhui, representatives Jiang Zhuoling, Chen Moquan, Zhang Jianqian, Shen Qingchan, County Magistrate of Fengxian, representatives He Zhiren, Zhang Xinjian, Ruan Xiyao, Jiang Wenhe, Zhu Ganye, Tao Jialin, and representatives of the 15 townships in the old Taiping Township of Nanhui, Pan Chengjiang and Yan Juting, totaling more than 20 people. First, the representatives of the two counties of Fengnan reported on their respective counties' recent claims regarding this case, and then the formal discussion began. As a result, the plan proposed by Nanhui County was adopted and supplemented, and five organizational proposals were formulated: 1. The 15 townships belonging to the old Taiping Township of Nanhui (i.e., part of the current tenth district) shall be designated as a unified autonomous region, and its district head shall be appointed by Nanhui County in accordance with the law after being recommended by Fengxian. 2. The Nanhui Puhan section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road (i.e., from Minhang opposite Puqi to the Gumutang Feng territory) within three li east and west shall be allocated to Fengxian for management. All police power in this section and criminal cases occurring in this section, as reported by the public security authorities in this section, shall be handled by Fengxian's administrative and judicial authorities. 3. Fengxian and Nanhui should organize a permanent dredging committee to handle the dredging of various trunk rivers in Fengxian that flow through Nanhui Jiang Taiping Heng Township and exit Pu. Fengxian shall account for two-thirds of the total number of members of the committee, and Nanhui shall account for one-third. The chairman of the committee shall be appointed by Fengxian. The expenses shall be allocated according to the length of the river, with equal distribution of land and labor. 4. Other construction and education matters related to the two counties shall also be handled in accordance with the above principles. 5. Nanhui Hall shall design and implement measures to benefit the people of the old Taiping Township as much as possible, such as setting up a branch for collecting land taxes in the area.

Wuxi

Provisional Measures for Agricultural Warehouse Mortgage 77

Wuxi: In order to alleviate the rural economic crisis, the People's Bank is preparing to establish rural storage and mortgage warehouses. Five locations have been set up initially and have already begun accepting mortgage goods and providing loans. Now, the Provincial Agricultural Bank, aiming to promote this system throughout the province, has specially formulated eight provisional measures to be distributed to various county branches for compliance. The measures are as follows: (1) In order to regulate food supply and support the rural economy, in addition to the warehouses operated by various branches, the bank may cooperate with rice-producing counties in the province that deem it necessary to implement rice mortgage programs. (2) Under the aforementioned cooperative arrangement, counties intending to implement rice mortgage programs should possess suitable buildings, recommend responsible personnel, and notify the bank with a letter, as well as raise a sufficient amount of capital (at least 20,000 yuan) to be deposited with the bank. The bank will then double the received amount as cooperative capital. (3) After the warehouse is established, the Agricultural Bank will be responsible for receipts, disbursements, and accounting, while the local authorities will be responsible for management and safekeeping. Monthly reports should be submitted, but for clarity, both parties may conduct audits at any time to ensure transparency. (4) When recovering principal and interest, the funds from the Agricultural Bank's capital portion should be repaid first. (5) Farmers mortgaging goods to the warehouse will be calculated at 60% of the market price, and the monthly interest rate shall not exceed 1%. Handling fees and other expenses may be added based on local conditions. (6) The funds provided by local authorities shall accrue interest at a monthly rate of 8 per mille. At the end of the program, any surplus, after deducting expenses, shall be used for local public welfare. (7) The rice mortgaged by farmers should be limited to their own produce. The mortgage procedures shall follow the bank's warehouse procedures. (8) These measures shall be applicable before January of the 22nd year [of the Republic, i.e., 1933].

Expanding the Anti-Drug Campaign 78

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, the County Party Headquarters convened a preparatory meeting for the anti-drug campaign, gathering representatives from various government agencies, organizations, and schools. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Appointed Zhang Zheng, Zhou Erkai, Shi Qinglin, Rui Lin, and Sun Chunpu as propaganda committee members. (2) Appointed Zhang Zheng as the propaganda team leader, and Zou Tingliang, Zhang Yuqing, Hua Qinda, Shen Xiang, Qin Songshi, Zhou Songshi, and Chen Yixin as propaganda team members. (3) Approved the anti-drug campaign promotion week plan. (4) Designated December 12th to 17th as anti-drug promotion week. (5) During the anti-drug promotion week, extensively recruit anti-drug comrades to join the anti-drug association. A general oath-taking ceremony will be held on the last day of the promotion week. After the promotion week, a formal inaugural meeting of the Wuxi Anti-Drug Association will be held. The responsibility for future anti-drug efforts will be entirely handed over to the Anti-Drug Association for long-term implementation. (6) During the anti-drug week, each school and social education institution will choose a time each day to give a speech on anti-drug issues. The materials will be provided by the County Party Headquarters.

Crackdown on Wuxi-Cheng Business Vehicles 79

The business vehicles on the Wuxi-Cheng road, with the construction office ordering the Wuxi and Cheng county construction bureaus, have agreed upon a compromise to restore traffic, following the regulations allowing only eight vehicles per day. However, in practice, the traffic remains as frequent as before. Recently, due to the obstruction of road construction, workers are unable to work more than four hours a day due to avoiding vehicles, making it impossible to achieve the original plan of transporting 30 cubic meters of materials per day. After approval from the Construction Department, the long-distance bus company ordered the Wuxi and Cheng county magistrates to strictly crack down on the business vehicles, prohibiting them from driving on the section in order to ensure the completion of the road construction project as scheduled.

Changzhou

Two Bandits Sentenced to Execution by Shooting 80

The Wuyi County Government has captured and brought before the court bandits Feng Abao and Cheng Yigen. After interrogation, they confessed to having committed robbery and kidnapping. They were sentenced to death, and the sentence was submitted to the provincial government for review. On the evening of the 9th, approval was received. Magistrate Zhang immediately dispatched police on the morning of the 10th to bring the bandits Feng Abao and Cheng Yigen to the execution ground outside Bo'ai Gate to verify their identities and carry out the execution by shooting.

Chenxiang Temple Robbed; Abbot Injured 81

Chenxiang Temple in Xiaorenqing, the fifteenth district of Wuyi, was suddenly attacked by armed bandits at approximately 3:00 AM on the 8th. They robbed important ornaments and severely burned the abbot, Yingxue, with fire, before fleeing after about an hour. Afterward, District Chief Zhang Renhe reported the case to the county government on the 9th.

Changshu

Flower Merchants Oppose Business Tax 82

Shazhou City in the fourth district of this county is mostly sandy land, and the villagers mainly grow cotton. Therefore, every autumn harvest, various yarn factories come to Xigang Changyinsha to set up cotton collection points to purchase cotton. Furthermore, due to the abundant harvest this year, there are more than twenty cotton collection points. However, regarding the business tax, the yarn factories have already determined the tax amount, and the cotton collection points are included. Now, the Business Tax Bureau of this county still requires each location to report and acknowledge the tax amount. As a result, the factories are jointly requesting instructions from the Department of Finance. Unexpectedly, the other day (the 7th), Gu Haoran from the Business Tax Bureau in the city was dispatched to the countryside to collect taxes. Because the instructions from the Department of Finance had not yet been reviewed, each location was unwilling to comply and pay, leading to a conflict in words. The manager of the Yikang Cotton Collection Point in Changyinsha was arrested. The cotton collection points, believing that the Business Tax Bureau officials had arrested someone without cause, jointly closed the market and stopped collecting cotton.

Nantong

Security Precautions on Land and Water in Tonghai and Qidong 83

Nantong County Magistrate Zhang Jian, Haimen County Magistrate Zhang Weixian, Qidong County Magistrate Fei Gongxia, and Provincial Water Police District Chief Zhang Xianyi jointly issued a proclamation on the 9th, implementing land and water security precautions against bandits. The coastal areas of Jiangbei and various ports on the north bank of the Yangtze River and the south bank of Changyinsha were separately sealed off and patrolled by stationed troops. Wooden sheds were set up at key land passages, stipulated to be closed every night at 9:00 PM and opened the next morning at 6:00 AM. Regarding anti-banditry matters, a guerrilla team was separately organized to handle them.

Four Central Committee Members, Including Deng Qingyang, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Will Travel to the Capital Tonight to Attend the Plenary Session; Joint Proposal Focuses on Resistance Against Japan and Suppression of Bandits 84

Four individuals, including Deng Qingyang, an alternate supervisory committee member of the Central Committee; Li Qian'an; and alternate executive committee members Guan Suren and Cui Guangxi, arrived in Shanghai on the 7th aboard the French postal ship "Qin Neng Su" from Hong Kong. The ship docked at the Huangpu Wharf in Tilanqiao at 10:00 AM yesterday. They disembarked around 11:00 AM. A reporter from the Central News Agency met with Committee Members Deng and Guan on board the ship yesterday and inquired about the date of their trip to the capital and the contents of their proposals. They provided detailed answers.

(Deng Qingyang said) Most of the Guangdong members were unable to attend the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee due to their official duties. I, along with Li Qian'an, Guan Suren, and Cui Guangxi, are relatively free, so we came to Shanghai specifically to travel to the capital and attend. However, regardless of whether they attend or not, all unanimously hope that the Central Committee can take responsibility and work hard to cope with the current national crisis. When I passed through Hong Kong on my way to Shanghai, I met with Mr. Hu Zhantang. Mr. Hu believed that it was impossible to force anyone to attend, but it was a good thing to be able to go to the capital and attend. Although Mr. Hu himself cannot attend due to illness, he did not give us any proposals to bring to the capital. However, Mr. Hu also holds the same hope, that the Central Committee can take responsibility and work hard to cope with the current national crisis. Rumors that Mr. Hu advocated not attending are inaccurate. The Guangdong authorities are currently working hard on construction, and the anti-Japanese sentiment among the people is extremely strong. The work of anti-Japanese organizations is very active, but it does not descend into clamor. Currently, Japanese goods have almost disappeared from the Guangzhou market. It is said that in North China and the Yangtze River area, Japanese goods are rampant, which is vastly different from Guangdong. I deeply hope that the anti-Japanese movement across the country will adopt the same pace as Guangdong, so that we can defeat the enemy and it is within our grasp. I am scheduled to take the night train to the capital with Mr. Li Qian'an on the 11th to attend the plenary session of the Supervisory Committee on the 12th. As for the proposals for the Third Plenary Session, I and Committee Members Li and Cui have already drafted a general proposal, which we will jointly submit to the plenary session for discussion, while my personal proposal is still being prepared.

(Guan Suren said) Among the Guangdong Committee members attending this Third Plenary Session, in addition to myself and Deng, Li, and Cui, there are several others who will come later, but the number is not large. I and Committee Members Deng, Li, and Cui have now drafted a proposal that we will jointly submit to the Third Plenary Session for discussion. The content focuses on actively resisting Japan and vigorously suppressing bandits. In addition, there will be criticism of the report of the League of Nations investigation team, and we will ask the Central Committee to instruct our representatives to the League of Nations to adopt a tough stance, to be unyielding, and to fight to the end. I have not met with the four Central Committee members Bai Wenwei, Zhang Zhiben, Liu Luyin, and Cheng Qian on this trip to Guangdong. I will stay in Shanghai for about one or two days, or will travel to the capital with Committee Member Deng and others tomorrow night (i.e., tonight).

(Cui Guangxi said) According to Mr. Cui Guangxi, speaking to a reporter from the New Voice Agency, they have not yet drafted any proposals and plan to draft them before entering the capital. The main points will be about how to thoroughly implement resistance against Japan and suppression of the communists. They cannot accept most of the International Investigation Team's report. They will have a meeting with Sun Zhesheng and other committee members tonight (i.e., last night) to finalize the proposals. They may add their names to Mr. Sun's proposal. Hu Zhantang has decided not to attend due to illness. Mr. Hu has been aging rapidly recently. He shares the same views as the other committee members regarding the proposals for resisting Japan and suppressing bandits at the Third Plenary Session. Liu Luyin also intends to come to Shanghai, but it is not yet known whether he can arrive before the meeting. In addition, Guangdong Committee members Wang Fangfu and Zhan Juci, as well as Guangxi Committee members Huang Xuchu and Li Renren, will continue to come to Shanghai and are expected to arrive here within about two days.

Li Jishen Leaves Shanghai

For Change of Scenery for Health; Requests Removal From All Concurrent Positions 85

Training Director Li Jishen asked for leave due to illness a month ago and came to Shanghai for treatment. Recently, he has not yet recovered, so he moved from his residence to a Western sanatorium on the Great West Road, where he was examined by Dr. Elster and his stool was tested by the Central Testing Laboratory. Many worm eggs were found, so it was said that these worms originated in the liver and affected the skin, so he often felt itchy all over and could not sleep at night. The doctor forbade him from eating meat and only allowed him to eat three thin slices of toast with each meal. He received an injection once a day. Although this had some effect after about two weeks, the doctor said that it was still advisable to move to another place for treatment. Coincidentally, his son, Peiwen, and daughter, Xiaomei, graduated from their studies in the United States and returned home via Europe. They should arrive in Hong Kong within a few days. Li loved his children, so he decided to return to Hong Kong first, partly to change scenery for health and partly to meet his children. Therefore, he boarded a certain postal ship yesterday to go abroad. It is said that before his departure, he telegraphed the Central Executive Committee and Chairman Chiang, and the original text is as follows: "To the Central Executive Committee in the capital: The Third Plenary Session is about to open. I hope that comrades will unite sincerely and jointly overcome the national crisis. Jishen is untalented and ashamed that he cannot participate in the grand event due to his long illness. Recently, according to the German doctor, the illness originates from the liver and appears on the skin. It will not be easy to achieve results without a change of scenery for treatment. I will buy a boat and return to my hometown immediately. I specially telegraph to ask for leave. Please understand. Li Jishen respectfully seals. To Chairman Chiang in Hankou and Nanjing: Jishen asked for leave last month to go to Shanghai for medical treatment due to illness. After a long time, he has not yet recovered. Recently, Dr. De was invited to examine him and said that the illness originates from the liver and appears on the skin. It will not be easy to achieve results without a change of scenery for treatment in a short time. Jishen has devoted himself to the party and the country, but he cannot make up for his difficulties, and he is plagued by the disease demon. What can I say? I have to submit a report to the National Government immediately, requesting to be removed from all concurrent positions and return to my hometown to recuperate in peace. I respectfully report this. I will continue to report the rest. Li Jishen respectfully seals."
