The Drawing for Principal Repayment of Seven Types of Public Bonds, Including Austrian Indemnity Bonds, Was Held Yesterday

A Total of 1,824,000 Yuan; Austria Will Pay the Remaining Amount at the End of the Month on the 20th 87

The eighth principal repayment of the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bills, the twelfth principal repayment of the Sixth Percent Public Bond of the Seventh Year of the Republic, the twelfth principal repayment of the Fourteenth Year of the Republic Public Bond, the eighth principal repayment of the Military Needs Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government, the eleventh principal repayment of the Post-War Short-Term Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government, the tenth principal repayment of the Disaster Relief Public Bond of the Eighteenth Year of the Republic, and the eighth principal repayment of the Customs Duty Public Bond of the Nineteenth Year of the Republic was held at 10:00 AM yesterday at the auditorium of the Bankers' Association at No. 4 Hong Kong Road. Representatives from the Ministry of Finance, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the National Debt Fund Management Committee, the Bankers' Association, and others were present.

(Chairman's Report) Zheng Lai, Director of the Public Debt Department, reported: "Today is the date for the principal repayment drawing of seven types of bonds, including the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bills. I am honored that you have come to observe. Now I will briefly report the details of the various bonds to you all. (1) The Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bills were issued in the fifteenth year of the Republic, with a total amount of 2.4 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid seven times. This is the eighth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be 24,000 yuan. (2) The Sixth Percent Public Bond of the Seventh Year of the Republic was issued with a total amount of 45 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid eleven times. This is the twelfth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be 450,000 yuan. (3) The Fourteenth Year of the Republic Public Bond was issued with a total amount of 15 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid eleven times. This is the twelfth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be 150,000 yuan. (4) The Military Needs Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government was issued in the seventeenth year of the Republic, with a total amount of 10 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid seven times. This is the eighth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be approximately 100,000 yuan. (5) The Post-War Short-Term Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government was issued in the seventeenth year of the Republic, with a total amount of 40 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid ten times. This is the eleventh principal repayment, with two winning tickets drawn, and the principal repayment should be 80 yuan. (6) The Disaster Relief Public Bond of the Eighteenth Year of the Republic was issued with a total amount of 10 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid nine times. This is the tenth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be 100,000 yuan. (7) The Customs Duty Public Bond of the Nineteenth Year of the Republic was issued with a total amount of 20 million yuan. Principal has already been repaid seven times. This is the eighth principal repayment, with one winning ticket drawn, and the principal repayment should be approximately 200,000 yuan. The above-mentioned winning bonds, except for the Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bills, which are scheduled to begin paying on December 20th, the remaining six types of bonds are scheduled to begin paying on December 31st. All the winning bonds should be paid with the principal by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in various places, together with the matured interest of each bond. Please have the supervisors verify the winning tickets and the register of winning tickets for the execution of the drawing."

(Winning Numbers) After the Chairman finished his report, the supervisors verified the winning tickets and the register of winning tickets, and then the drawers executed the drawing. The winning numbers are as follows: (1) Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed 24 Treasury Bills, one ticket: "No. 18"; (2) Sixth Percent Public Bond of the Seventh Year of the Republic, one ticket: "No. 56"; (3) Fourteenth Year of the Republic Public Bond, one ticket: "No. 11"; (4) Military Needs Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance, one ticket: "No. 59"; (5) Post-War Short-Term Public Bond of the Ministry of Finance, two tickets: "No. 16," "No. 86"; (6) Disaster Relief Public Bond of the Eighteenth Year of the Republic, one ticket: "No. 85"; (7) Customs Duty Public Bond of the Nineteenth Year of the Republic, one ticket: "No. 60." The total principal repayment for the above seven types of public bonds is approximately 1,824,000 yuan.

The Standing Committee Meeting of the Association for the Abolition of Civil War Resolved to Announce Non-Cooperation with Liu Xiang

Telegraphic Petition from Representatives to the Third Plenary Session Requesting Central Government to Severely Punish Liu Xiang 88

The General Association for the Abolition of Internal Warfare held its third executive committee meeting yesterday at 2:00 PM. Thirty-seven executive committee members attended. Wang Xiaolai was unanimously elected as temporary chairman, and Gu Huaibing served as secretary. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

(Executive Committee Members Present) Qian Xinzhi, Wu Daquan, (Qian Xinzhi substituting for) Du Yuesheng, Lu Runquan, Pu Xinya, (Lu Runquan substituting for) Wang Xiaolai, Jin Runquan, Song Yuting, (Wang Xiaolai substituting for) Chen Liting, Zhou Zuomin, (Chen Liting substituting for), Chen Peide, Leng Zhanqi, (Qi Yunqing substituting for) Yang Meizhen, Li Gongpu, Hu Shuhua, Fu Yueqi, (Hu Shuhua substituting for) Li Denghui, Bei Songsun, Liu Shimu, Wang Yansong, Lin Kanghou, Yu Xiaochuan, Xu Huaiqing, Wang Yiling, Li Kuian, (Lin Kanghou substituting for) Yan Esheng, Yu Rongqiao, Lin Junbao, (Yan Esheng substituting for) Liu Zhanen, Chen Shi, Ma Wenhui, (Liu Zhanen substituting for) Xu Jilou, Chen Zhezheng, (Xu Jilou substituting for) Lu Zhangyuan, Yu Dichen, Zhou Xuexiang, Zhu Xuefan

(Meeting Proceedings) At 2:30 PM, the number of executive committee members present reached the legal quorum, and the meeting was declared open. The temporary chairman respectfully read the will of the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen, followed by a report on the number of attendees. Next, Secretary-General Yan Esheng reported on the telegram from Mr. Yu Rizhang from Geneva and on the association's work. In addition to distributing printed materials, he detailed the achievements since the association's founding and the anti-internal warfare movement in Sichuan Province. Subsequently, Xu Jilou, representing treasurer Chen Zhezheng, reported on the association's income and expenditures, and distributed financial reports. The temporary chairman then reported on the progress of contacting and organizing branch associations in Wuhan. Yan Esheng, representing Bao Ling, reported on the establishment and work of the Tianjin branch association. Hu Shuhua reported on the methods for organizing branch associations in Hunan Province. After the reports, the discussion of proposals began.

(Work Achievements) Secretary-General Yan Esheng reported on the work achievements, stating: "The association was formally established only three months ago, and branch associations have not yet been widely established in various locations. The number of members has also not reached the maximum. With an organization that is not yet fully sound, we have taken on the arduous task of abolishing internal warfare. Furthermore, we encountered the Shandong Incident, followed by internal warfare in Sichuan and Guizhou provinces. I am ashamed that we have not been able to achieve our ideal and satisfactory goal of eliminating and preventing these conflicts, and that we have failed to live up to the expectations of the people of the country. However, arduous tasks cannot be accomplished overnight, and effective methods require collective efforts. Although the association's past work has not had a significant practical effect, it has had a substantial spiritual impact. Acting Premier Song Ziwen's speech on November 6th indicated that outstanding individuals in the country have organized the 'General Association for the Abolition of Internal Warfare,' and its influence is growing stronger daily, soon becoming an important force in abolishing the use of force to resolve political issues." This speech has been widely reported in foreign newspapers, and can greatly attract international attention. Regarding the recently concluded Shandong Han-Liu conflict, Mr. Zhang Boling, a member of this association's executive committee, reported from Shanghai that the fact that the conflict was not extremely fierce was partly due to the repeated dissuasion by this association. As for the Sichuan conflict, this association received reports from Sichuanese people in Shanghai in September of this year, stating that Chengdu and Chongqing were making military movements and that unfortunate events were likely to occur. They requested that measures be taken to eliminate the conflict. Considering the pressing national crisis, how could internal strife be tolerated, this association immediately telegraphed Liu Wenhui in Chengdu and Liu Xiang in Chongqing, requesting them to reply swiftly to reassure the people. At the same time, we telegraphed the chambers of commerce in Chengdu and Chongqing to inquire about the truth and to eliminate the conflict as appropriate. Subsequently, we received a telegram from Liu Wenhui stating, "We are preoccupied with resisting foreign aggression and cannot bear to speak of private fights. Wenhui is internally seeking cooperation and is willing to yield to others. This has always been my intention, and God is my witness. Even if people do not conspire with me, I will strive to avoid conflict. While I can compromise, I will never initiate conflict," and so on. We also received a telegram from Liu Xiang stating, "The officers and soldiers in Sichuan are thinking of sharpening their swords and preparing their horses to support the government's diplomacy. How can they kill each other and lightly start war? The military actions you inquired about are all under my command. The so-called 'idle talk' may not satisfy everyone's hearts, but it intends to provoke discord," and so on. In early October, due to more urgent rumors, this association telegraphed both sides again, urging them to quickly order their troops not to act rashly. Soon after sending the telegram, we received a reply telegram from Liu Wenhui stating that he would "not hesitate to make every effort to resolve the dispute internally, hoping that those who cause chaos will realize their mistakes, so as not to betray the sincere teachings," and so on. However, there was no reply from Liu Xiang. Before long, the Sichuan war broke out. This association repeatedly tried to stop it, but to no avail. On November 23, we received another telegram from Liu Wenhui, stating the process of his retreat, voluntarily giving up defenses in various places, hoping for the vindication of justice and a quick resolution of the dispute. This association then telegraphed the Military Affairs Commission and the Ministry of Military Administration of the National Government again, requesting them to strictly order the generals on all sides to strictly order their subordinates to abide by the National Government's order to cease fire immediately, and to ask Liu Xiang to express his agreement with the peaceful proposition and jointly plan concrete measures to resolve the dispute and reorganize Sichuan's administration. After the telegram was sent, we received a reply from the Military Affairs Commission stating that the resolution of the Sichuan war was being planned, but we still did not receive any response from Liu Xiang. Recent news reports indicate that Liu Xiang still plans to launch a general offensive against Liu Wenhui at a fixed time, which shows where the failure to stop the Sichuan war lies. Furthermore, as reported by the local newspapers, a telegram from Chengdu on November 2 stated that students from Rongchang Municipal Elementary School formed an anti-war propaganda team and went to various villages to spread their message. Yesterday, at Wanbao Fang, seven people were arrested by Battalion Commander Huang of Wang Zanxu's troops of the Chongqing army and sent to the command headquarters. The leading student, Shen Xuanheng, was accused of inciting the troops and was immediately executed. The others are under interrogation. Not only that, but a Chongqing telegram on December 2 reported that the Xinshu Daily was sealed by the Garrison Command for publishing the National Government's order to cease fire. Later, due to the intercession of a certain important person, the person in charge of the newspaper wrote a letter of repentance and the matter was settled. This shows that Liu Xiang not only suppressed the people's anti-internal warfare movement, but also defied the National Government's cease-fire order. A Chongqing telegram on the same day stated that Lan Wenbin, a brigade commander of the 21st Army, was detained for 20 days for opposing the war. On the morning of December 1, Liu Xiang telegraphed the military headquarters to have Lan executed by firing squad. Another telegram stated that the Chongqing business community's opposition to the third phase of financial bonds was expanding. Yutong Bank, whose capital was known to be strong, was closed by the authorities, and the manager was detained in the Garrison Command. The bank's cash was confiscated. More than a dozen small money shops and foreign goods stores in Chongqing were affected and closed down, and cries of distress were heard everywhere. Article 2, Section 3 of this association's charter stipulates that if internal warfare unfortunately occurs, the association's member organizations and individual members should unanimously refuse to cooperate and should adopt peaceful and appropriate methods to stop it. Therefore, when the Sichuan war was raging, the Sichuan branch of this association was established in Chongqing on October 16, and issued a public statement, clearly stating that it would not comply with any conscription. Prior to this, the Chongqing Municipal Department and Association also replied to the initial telegram from this association inquiring about the situation in Sichuan, stating, "At this time of crisis, we must revitalize the spirit of the anti-internal warfare movement. We must refuse to comply with any conscription, except for the usual regular supplies." Therefore, the Chongqing business community's refusal to purchase the third phase of financial bonds is not unconnected to this association's spirit of non-cooperation with those who wage internal warfare. At the same time, the Chengdu Chamber of Commerce replied to this association's telegram on October 10, stating, "Rather than lingering in a dying state, it is better to cut off the root of the problem. We will lead hundreds of thousands of merchants in the city to follow behind." Currently, various groups in Chengdu have organized the People's Anti-War Alliance to support peace and stop the chaotic war. The Chengdu Chamber of Commerce has also issued a declaration requesting the complete withdrawal of troops from the city. If this goal is not achieved, they will resist by striking to achieve their goals. The Sichuan branch of this association, as well as the business community, financial community, academia, and other people's organizations in Chengdu and Chongqing, are all willing to sacrifice everything to oppose internal warfare. This spirit and courage are truly admirable."

(Resolutions) ㈠ Discussing the proposal to petition the Third Plenary Session to stop internal warfare and unite against foreign aggression: The Third Plenary Session is scheduled to be held in Beijing on the 15th of this month. This association should petition the plenary session to resolve to stop internal warfare and unite against foreign aggression to save the country. Is this appropriate? Please decide. Resolution: Passed. Pu Yangshan, Liu Zhanen, and Lin Kanghou were unanimously elected as representatives to present the petition. ㈡ Discussing the proposal to universally solicit members: To strengthen the association's power, it is necessary to universally solicit members. Members from all sectors, including agriculture, industry, commerce, and academia, are welcome to join. In particular, we hope that former officers and personnel who have served in the military and political fields will join this association to guide our work and to express their determination not to participate in internal warfare in the future. Is this appropriate? Please decide. ㈢ Discussing the proposal for chambers of commerce in provinces and cities to organize anti-internal warfare committees before branch associations are established: According to the regulations of this association, the organization of branch associations should be handled by representatives from local legal organizations. However, the procedures cannot be completed in a short time, and we must strive for thoroughness in the process. Before branch associations are established in various places, should chambers of commerce first establish anti-internal warfare committees within their associations to communicate and facilitate progress? Is this appropriate? Please decide. The above two proposals were discussed together. Resolution: A telegram will be sent to chambers of commerce in various provinces and cities to organize anti-internal warfare committees, to universally solicit members in accordance with the association's purpose, and then to plan the organization of branch associations. ㈣ Discussing the Sichuan internal warfare case: The two main parties involved in the Sichuan war are Liu Wenhui and Liu Xiang. Liu Wenhui has already issued a statement declaring his retreat and expressing his willingness to cease fire. This association has also telegraphed Liu Xiang, requesting him to comply with the central government's order and quickly cease fire, but we have not yet received a reply. What further actions should this association take to effectively stop the war? Please decide. Resolution: (A) Announce Liu Xiang's violation of the National Government's order, continuing internal warfare, closing newspapers and banks, and committing the crimes of executing Lan Wenbin, a brigade commander who opposed internal warfare, and Shen Xuanheng, a student at Rongchang Municipal Elementary School. (B) Submit a petition to the central government to severely punish Liu Xiang. (C) Contact Sichuanese people and business organizations in Shanghai to plan methods to stop the war. (D) Send a telegram to the entire country to not cooperate with Liu Xiang. ㈤ Discussing the Guizhou internal warfare case: This association telegraphed the Guiyang County Chamber of Commerce to inquire about the details of the Guizhou internal warfare and to eliminate the conflict as appropriate, but we have not yet received a reply. How should we plan methods to stop the conflict? Please decide. Resolution: Send a telegram urging the Guiyang County Chamber of Commerce to reply quickly, and unite with Guizhou people in Shanghai to plan effective methods to stop the conflict. ㈥ Discussing effective and proactive methods to abolish internal warfare: The steps this association takes to abolish internal warfare are: first, persuasion; second, sending representatives to mediate; and third, non-cooperation. However, based on past experience, the first two steps, while not completely ineffective, have yielded very little. How should the third step be implemented, and are there any other effective methods? Please decide. Resolution: Implement non-cooperation with those who wage internal warfare, and expand publicity. ㈦ Discussing the budget: The expenditure budget approved by the second executive committee meeting was for a three-month trial period. Now that the trial period has expired, should we continue to operate according to it, or should we revise it? Please decide. Resolution: Continue the trial operation for three months. ㈧ Discussing the date and location of the next executive committee meeting: Article 7 of the executive committee regulations stipulates that the executive committee shall hold a regular meeting once every three months, and the date and location of the next regular meeting shall be decided by the previous executive committee meeting. Please decide. Resolution: To be held in Tianjin in March of the 22nd year [of the Republic], the date to be decided by the executive committee on duty. ㈨ Discussing the term of office and re-election methods for executive committee members of branch associations: The regulations of this association's branch associations do not clearly stipulate the term of office and re-election methods for executive committee members of branch associations. Please discuss and decide. Resolution: The term of office and re-election methods for executive committee members of branch associations shall be handled in accordance with Article 6 of the general association's charter. ㈩ Discussing the temporary proposals of Executive Committee Member Chen Peide: (A) Expand publicity methods. Resolution: Handled by the executive committee on duty. (B) Advise national people's organizations to participate in the abolition of war. Resolution: To be handled together with the second and third items of the resolution. ㈩㈠ Discussing the temporary proposal of Executive Committee Member Hu Shuhua: Send a telegram to soldiers across the country to inspire their conscience, unite against foreign aggression, and recover lost territory. Resolution: Passed.

Today's Memorial Service for Martyred Boy Scouts of the Chamber of Commerce

Simultaneous Ceremonies Held in Beiping, Guangdong, Hankou, etc. Chamber of Commerce Cables Representatives in Geneva to Appeal 92

The four martyrs, Boy Scouts Luo Yunxiang and others of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, sacrificed their lives for the country during the January 28th Incident when Japanese troops invaded Shanghai. A memorial service will be held specifically this afternoon at 2:00 PM in the auditorium of the Chamber of Commerce near the Tianhou Palace Bridge. The Chamber of Commerce especially telegraphed the Chinese delegation in Geneva, requesting a report to the world. Memorial services are also being held simultaneously in Beiping, Guangdong, Hankou, and other locations. Details are recorded as follows:

Holding Memorial Service 93

The medal presentation ceremony for the four martyrs of the Chamber of Commerce Boy Scouts, Luo Yunxiang, Bao Zhengwu, Mao Weixiang, and Ying Wenda, who died in the line of duty, will be presided over by Xu Wencheng. The chairman of the memorial service is Tong Xingbai, and the chairman of the unveiling ceremony for the monument is Wang Xiaolai. The Shanghai Boy Scout Council received a telegram yesterday from the Preparatory Office of the General Association of Boy Scouts of China, stating: ㈠ Upon the order of the Chairman, Secretary Teng Jie is assigned to represent the association in posthumously awarding honorary medals to the four martyred Boy Scouts and to participate in the memorial service. ㈡ Section Chief Xu Guanyu is assigned to represent the preparatory office in attending the memorial service.

Welcoming Representatives 94

Teng Jie, Secretary, representing Chairman Chiang Kai-shek of the General Association of Boy Scouts of China, and Xu Guanyu, representative of the Preparatory Office of the General Association, arrived in Shanghai by the Beijing-Shanghai express train at 5:00 PM yesterday. Xu Guozhi, commander of the 50th Boy Scout Corps, led the entire corps to welcome them at the North Railway Station. As for Hankou, the memorial service was initiated by the municipal party department. In Beiping, it was initiated by the Boy Scout Self-Help Society. In Guangdong, it was initiated by the 48th Boy Scout Corps. All held simultaneous memorial services today for the four martyred Boy Scouts, Luo Yunxiang and others.

Requesting an Appeal by Telegram 95

(Omitted above) To the Chinese Delegation in Geneva: During the anti-Japanese resistance in Shanghai, the 50th Boy Scout Corps of China (Troop Fifty Boy Scouts of China), organized by this association, dispatched four Boy Scouts, Luo Yunxiang, Bao Zhengwu, Mao Weixiang, and Ying Wenda, wearing red cross armbands, to go deep into the war zone with members of the Red Cross Society to rescue the suffering people. However, they were captured by the Japanese army. Refugees who escaped and were acquainted with the four corps members reported that they had seen them being tied up by the Japanese awaiting execution. After the efforts of the Public Concession Bureau and consuls of various countries to rescue them, the Japanese initially prevaricated, and then claimed that there were no such people, as they had already been killed, their bodies destroyed, and the evidence erased, the same as the Cai Gongshi case of the previous year, after which they made excuses. Now, at the time of the League of Nations meeting, we are using this to present the Japanese's disregard for international law to the world, hoping that it will receive the same attention as the recent massacre of civilians in Fushun. Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce.

Declaration of the Assembly 96

The declaration of the memorial service for the four martyred Boy Scouts of Songhu states: After the January 28th battle, the history of Chinese Boy Scouts has a more glorious and moving page. The fact is that the cruel and war-loving Japan was coveting the fertile Northeast and, under the pretext of self-defense, forcibly occupied it. Not satisfied with that, it sent barbaric troops to ravage Shanghai. Its intention was nothing more than to divert the world's attention, in order to secretly complete the preliminary plan of its decades-long conspiracy: to establish a puppet state. The loyal 19th Route Army and the 5th Army, etc., in order to uphold human justice and seek the survival of the nation, disregarded everything and rose up to resist. At the same time, our Boy Scouts, seeing countless compatriots being innocently massacred, driven by a sense of responsibility, and based on the second article of the Boy Scout Oath: to help others at all times and serve the public, abandoned their personal careers and families and quickly organized a battlefield service group, assisting the Red Cross, risking life and limb in the midst of gunfire and bullets, and saving the lives of many suffering compatriots. Unfortunately, the four comrades of the 50th Corps, Luo Yunxiang, Ying Wenda, Bao Zhengwu, and Mao Weixiang, were thus captured and cruelly murdered by the Japanese invaders under the false accusation of being spies. The loyal remains have not yet been found. A Boy Scout without political colors, with the aim of seeking world peace, wearing the symbol of the Red Cross, which is not allowed to be hated by international law, was actually cruelly murdered. This is unprecedented. From this, it can be seen that the brutal Japan is not only the enemy of the Chinese people, but also the public enemy of all countries in the world. If world justice is to exist, then we must attack the Japanese people. Originally, the economies of various countries were struggling and unable to take care of their own affairs. How could they have the leisure to care about other people's affairs? After all, we are Chinese people, and we are interdependent. Therefore, the final victory still depends on self-reliance, self-encouragement, and striving to struggle. We must not shout slogans and whistle on paper, doing things that are useless in practice. Although the situation in Shanghai seems to have passed, with singing, dancing, and nightlife continuing, the ashes of the war zone are still exposed and have not been erased. The Northeast Volunteer Army is still using old weapons and wearing thin clothes, continuing the anti-Japanese work in the frozen wilderness. Therefore, our greatest task at present is to carry on the legacy of the martyrs, avenge the shame, and save the country. Even if we cannot hold a gun and go to the front line, we must at least do some work to help the wounded and save the dying, and serve humanity. We must carry forward the resolute spirit of the Boy Scouts. Wherever our duty lies, we will not hesitate to die. We feel deeply ashamed for living after the four comrades who died for their country. In addition to finding ways to provide compensation for the families of the martyrs, the 50th Corps has applied to the organizing agency, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, to build a memorial tower to commend the righteous army. In the future, it will be decided to build a cenotaph in the central area of Shanghai to ensure immortality. On the one hand, it can prevent the souls of the martyrs from having no place to rest, and on the other hand, it can give future generations admiration. Now, under the order of the General Association of Boy Scouts of China, the Shanghai Special Municipality Boy Scout Council is holding this grand memorial service. We are very grateful for the elegiac couplets and eulogies given by all walks of life. In the future, not only our Boy Scouts must always identify their goals and work hard, but we also hope that people from all walks of life will give us deeper sympathy and assistance, so that the legacy of the four martyrs can be extended, the great enemy of mankind can be eliminated, the nation can be saved from danger, and the world can achieve equality. This declaration is hereby made.

The 93-year-old Ma Xiangbo Advocated Raising Voluntary Donations for Righteous Soldiers

One Copper Coin Per Person Per Day 97

Ma Xiangbo, a ninety-three-year-old elder, expressed his views to a reporter from the New Voice Society yesterday on assisting the Northeast Volunteer Army, saying: Recent news indicates that General Su Bingwen led his troops to seek refuge in Russian territory. Japan regards this as a national criminal matter and demands extradition, viewing the three eastern provinces as the Emperor's land and not belonging to China. On one hand, they falsely claim popular will to establish a nation under Japanese supervision and management, attempting to deceive the world. On the other hand, they arbitrarily slaughter our compatriots, not valuing them as much as chickens or dogs. This is intolerable! How can this be tolerated? This is not treating our 470 million compatriots as human beings. Once they slaughter 470 million chickens and dogs, even humanity might find it unbearable. Therefore, in addition to various public donations and monthly contributions, I propose initiating a fundraising campaign for the Chinese Volunteer Donation, one copper coin per person per day, aiming to make our 470 million compatriots, who are suffering this unprecedented great shame and humiliation, feel ashamed and rise up, never forgetting day by day. Those who rise up are helped by Heaven, and those who feel ashamed are blessed by Heaven. What is most heartbreaking is that some countrymen are still killing each other, openly assisting the enemy, and others are passively watching the killings, secretly assisting the enemy. For the present plan, our people should only ask their conscience, protect their integrity, fulfill their national duty donation, and fulfill their national crisis special donation. Let me elaborate: The national duty donation means that among the 470 million citizens, deducting 70 million who are fighting and those who have been injured or disabled, there are still 400 million compatriots who contribute one copper coin per day, 360 copper coins per year, which is equivalent to one silver dollar. Even beggars can do it. This means that 400 million silver dollars can be donated in one year, which is more than 33 million silver dollars per month. It seems to be better than other donations that have no fixed amount or period, and its significance is more sufficient to awaken compatriots to be vigilant every day. One copper coin, one share, is the minimum requirement. What is the national crisis special donation? In this time of man-made disasters and natural calamities, the so-called imperialist conquest ideology treats our people as less than chickens and dogs. We must be insulted before others insult us, so we should save on luxury to supplement the insufficiency of the mandatory donations. The main items for saving are as follows: 1. Entertainment donation, referring to automatic donations of a certain amount in entertainment venues, or the method of levying entertainment tax can also be adopted. 2. Anti-drug donation, referring to eating one or two fewer simple meals every day, which benefits both people and oneself. Even a big [something is missing], why not do it? 3. Luxury donation, referring to using one less box or bottle of perfume and cologne per month, and wearing one less piece of Stanco foreign clothing. 4. Savings donation, referring to ordering one or two fewer dishes or eating one or two less items at home or when entertaining guests. 5. Tobacco and alcohol donation, referring to smoking one or two fewer cigarettes or drinking one or two fewer sips of foreign wine and sorghum liquor. 6. Buddhist donation, referring to doing merit deeds, such as burning incense and lighting candles on the first and fifteenth days of the lunar month, and burning incense and chanting Buddha in various temples, burning one less bundle of incense, lighting one less pair of candles, preparing one less vegetarian meal, and burning one less knife of tin foil. These kinds of righteous donations are truly great compassion, rescuing from suffering and difficulties. 7. Sutra and repentance donation, referring to performing one less ritual or reducing the scale of Taoist ceremonies, communal feasts, offering food to hungry ghosts, suppressing disasters, repenting before Buddha, and worshipping the stars every year, and using the savings for righteous donations, which will surely cultivate blessings, longevity, children, and grandchildren. In China, from ancient times to the present, officials take money, and the people give money. Empty-handed, without any achievements, Heaven sees that the people's weakness often leads to survival in hopeless situations, just as the Empress Dowager's tolerance of the Boxers led to the invasion of the Eight-Nation Alliance, yet our country did not perish. After the defeat of the Sino-Japanese War, Ito Hirobumi was extremely arrogant, but An Jung-geun assassinated him. When he was executed, he said to his younger brother, Jeong-geun, "My country's enemy is also China's enemy. I wish to die for the sake of relations between the two countries and the overall situation in East Asia. I hope the Chinese nation will understand my humble intentions and deeply consider the fate of the two countries to save my 20 million Koreans and 400 million Chinese people from the abyss of misery. I have something to say now: Unless Korean independence is restored, the Chinese nation will have no peace of mind." This prediction, which appeared in the first issue of the New Korean Youth magazine, has now been verified. It must be understood that Japan's invasion of the Northeast is the beginning of the conquest of China and the world, as seen in their memorials. However, Heaven loves life, and if we are willing to feel ashamed and rise up, we will never allow them to devour us. All hope lies in the cooperation of our compatriots in distress. Although the strategy is small, its function is vast. The method of raising funds is to have the leaders of each family, each household, each store, each institution, each group, business association, factory, school, etc., collect and store the funds. The method is to have the banks in each county publicly recommend and designate [someone]. Since this is initiated and donated by the people, it should all be discussed and used by the people, either to open factories to manufacture or to find ways to purchase guns, cannons, and airplanes, vowing not to recover the three northeastern provinces. Rather be shattered like jade than remain whole like tile.

Please Expedite the Resolution of the Outstanding Rent Reduction Case

The Cost of Living Index Has Fallen, but Rent Has Increased. If Administrative Measures Are Not Taken Soon, Businesses Will Be Forced to Liquidate and Close Down. 98

|| Citizen Association Re-Submits Document to the Municipal Party Headquarters ||

The Shanghai First Special Zone Citizens' Association previously submitted a request to the Municipal Party Headquarters, urging them to expedite the resolution of the outstanding rent reduction case. The Association received instructions yesterday and immediately submitted another urgent request. The correspondence is recorded below.

Instructions from the Municipal Party Headquarters 99

Received one document: Requesting expedited resolution of rent reduction to maintain commerce. The case was previously submitted to the Central Committee, which instructed the Executive Yuan to dispatch personnel to work with Party and government organs to revise the standard measures for rent reduction. Later, a reply was received from the Central Secretariat, stating that the Executive Yuan had responded to the Municipal Government of this city, stating that the previously established standard measures had been promulgated for a long time, and any easy changes might cause disputes. It is proposed that the Central Committee send personnel to Shanghai for investigation to clarify the truth. The Central Committee was then requested to send personnel to Shanghai to investigate and handle the matter. Please be informed. This order.

Petition from the Citizens' Association 100

Petition regarding the imminent end of the year and the need for rapid rent reduction to save businesses from bankruptcy and prevent long-term resistance. We respectfully received instruction No. 227 of the [department] (original text omitted above). According to the index table of Shanghai's cost of living issued by the National Tariff Commission, Volume 8, No. 10, October of the 21st year, the index for food was 122.8 in February and 94.9 in October; the index for clothing was 108.2 in February and 99.0 in October; the index for rent was 107.3 in February and 108.8 in October; the index for fuel was 141.4 in February and 131.7 in October; the index for miscellaneous items was 193.60 in February and 165.2 in October; the total index was 163.4 in February and 113.50 in October. In summary, the above indexes show that the prices of four items have fallen, and the price of food (mainly rice) has fallen the most, while rent has increased instead. This shows that real estate still utilizes semi-patents and has no alternatives, and cannot be arbitrarily abandoned at any time. If rent is not reduced, it will continue to increase. When rice prices rise, officials should immediately issue price limits to alleviate the living difficulties of civilians. If rent is not subject to administrative restrictions in peacetime, it is enough to make shopkeepers deliberately save on essential living expenses to pay for rent. Since the Shanghai turmoil caused by the violent Japanese, Shanghai's commerce has plummeted. Layoffs and salary cuts and [unclear] sales revenue are barely enough to cover rent expenses, and there is often a shortfall. It was originally hoped that rent reduction could be implemented early so that the pressure could be temporarily relieved in the autumn and winter seasons, and donations for rescuing refugees in the Northeast and assisting volunteer armies could be provided by citizens to relieve national crises. The duty must be fulfilled with effort, so the situation is even more strained. Please carefully examine the donations from Shanghai, the number of real estate holders who bear the burden, and what the statistics show. There has been criticism in the people's newspapers that it seems that the country can be lost, the land can be lost, but the rent increase cannot be stopped. If administrative measures are not taken early, there will be no one to supply the needs of long-term resistance. I fear that when the end of the year arrives, businesses will have a tendency to liquidate and close down, which will further increase the serious problem of [something]. It will be too late to remedy the situation at that time. The [Municipal Party Headquarters] is keenly aware of the commercial and industrial situation in Shanghai, and we have already received instructions to re-request the Central Committee, which we dare not repeatedly solicit. However, we are compelled by the need to look ahead and behind. We once again venture to trouble the [Municipal Party Headquarters] and humbly request that you expedite the submission to the Central Committee for instructions to the government to take rapid action to maintain the Shanghai commercial and industrial economy and facilitate long-term resistance. We are sincerely grateful.

Current Situation of Northeast Postal Services 101

According to the Central News Agency, a postal authority told reporters yesterday that since our three northeastern provinces were occupied by violent Japanese forces, all post offices and staff were withdrawn into the interior due to transportation obstructions. Only 26 post offices remained on both sides of Suifenhe in Jilin Province. The area is close to the Russian border and can be reached by sea via Vladivostok to connect with the provinces under the [Postal Service] Headquarters. As of now, no reports have been received, and there are no unexpected occurrences. As for the area where Su Bingwen's troops were stationed to resist the Japanese, it was in the Greater Khingan Mountains. Transportation was obstructed, so the post office had been withdrawn long ago. After Su's withdrawal, there was no connection with the postal service.

Statements from Financial Circles after E W Eames Defection

Damage to Credit of Foreign Employees in Various Institutions; Ample Reason to Seek Recovery of Pension 102

After local Chinese and foreign newspapers revealed that former Acting Inspector General of Customs E W Eames had accepted the position of customs advisor to the puppet Manchukuo regime, all customs personnel, both Chinese and foreign, expressed indignation. Chinese personnel believed that Eames's actions were ungrateful and disloyal, as he had been supported by China for decades. Foreign personnel believed that Eames's actions were detrimental to the reputation of foreigners and revealed that foreigners serving in the Chinese government lacked loyalty and integrity, which would affect the credibility of foreign employees serving in various institutions in China in the future. Therefore, at a banquet in financial circles the other day, a certain gentleman made a speech. However, the gentleman was a person in financial circles and not a customs officer. The reference to the staff of the Inspectorate General of Customs was a misrepresentation. At the request of the gentleman, a correction is made. After inquiring from various sources about Eames's past, it was confirmed that he had served in the Customs for more than 20 years and held a very high position. Even after the establishment of the National Government, he was promoted to the position of Acting Inspector General of Customs. Later, he retired due to old age and received a pension of more than 100,000 yuan. It was expected that he would retire and enjoy his old age without worrying about his livelihood. Now, he does not know how to cherish himself and relies on the puppet regime, which is a burden on his later years. The pension given by the Chinese government was originally intended for the support of employees after retirement due to old age. Now that Eames does not cherish his old age and willingly defects to the enemy, diplomatic negotiations should be conducted to recover the pension, which is a sufficient reason. Moreover, Eames is now openly active in Geneva as an advisor to the puppet state, which seems to place him in a position contrary to China. Therefore, if the Chinese government formally raises this point, it can also expose his fickleness.

I believe that the foreign guests present today are 120,000 percent sympathetic and are very willing to support [us] in the end. Chiang's Second Speech 104

Finally, Chiang stood up again and said: "Today, I am extremely grateful to have Chinese and foreign guests come to provide guidance. I would like to take this opportunity to say a few more words. There is an ancient Chinese saying: 'Floods and wild beasts' are the most harmful to the world's humanity. China is now a country with internal troubles and external threats, especially with the addition of the disaster of floods. Of course, the people suffer great pain, and the country faces endless dangers. Fortunately, enthusiastic patriots and friendly foreigners have in the past run around calling for help and assisting the government. I am extremely grateful and give them 120,000 thanks. I have one sentence to say to you, that is, even though we are in the midst of floods, wild beasts, internal troubles, and external threats, we will definitely be able to fight our way out and open up a path to life, and we will never betray your kindness. Now China is still in a precarious situation. Fortunately, disaster relief and bandit suppression have achieved good results, and the foundation for national salvation has been established. I firmly believe that in a year's time, we will be able to walk on the road to brightness. I especially hope that Chinese and foreign celebrities and people across the country will continue to cooperate with the government to the end to complete the task of saving the country and the people and increasing the happiness of mankind." After Chiang finished speaking, it was already 6 o'clock, and the gathering ended happily.

Banquet by Wuhan Municipal Government 105

The Hankou Municipal Government hosted a banquet for the Dike Project Inspection Group at the Yan Yip Bank on the second floor at 7:30 pm on the 4th. Mayor Wu Guozhen, Public Security Bureau Chief Chen Xizeng, and the head of the Municipal Government's Secretariat Section all came to greet the guests in person. During the banquet, Mayor Wu delivered a speech, saying: "I am very pleased to welcome the Dike Project Inspection Group from afar to Hankou. The repair of the Yangtze River dike has been completed, like a Great Wall. I have two thoughts: (1) The completion of this dike depends on foreign investment, American wheat, and the help of foreign talents such as Mr. Simpson, so the achievements are great and the completion is rapid. This point is enough to show that the construction of the new China is extremely in need of foreign capital and foreign talents. As long as foreign capital has no political effect and foreign talents are completely dedicated to China's construction, we are extremely welcome. It is definitely not like some people who promote in Europe that China is anti-foreign and rejects foreign investment. This point can be refuted without attacking. The second point is that the completion of this 3,000-mile dike is enough to show the efforts and concentration of the Chinese people. 1931 was an unfortunate year for the whole world, especially the most unfortunate year for China. We suffered internal floods and external aggression. Even in this difficult environment, the Chinese people are still constantly striving to complete the great dike project. Now that the dike project is completed, we hope to dredge the Yangtze River to avoid suffering from floods in the future. I hope that everyone present will assist in the progress. Otherwise, the dike project cannot be permanently kept safe, just as the Great Wall cannot permanently resist the invasion of the Xiongnu." Next, [something] by

[P Simpson's Reply]

Stating, "During this inspection of the dike project, one shortcoming in Hankou was noted, namely that half a mile of the riverbank in the Japanese concession has not been built with a flood control dike, which is regrettable. If this small section is not built, Hankou's flood control dike is equivalent to a mere formality. I hope the mayor will negotiate with the Japanese side to explain the advantages and disadvantages and complete it according to the plan. In addition, regarding China's hopes, the Chinese people must recognize that everyone is Chinese, and there should be no distinctions between provinces, especially in times of national crisis. All domestic undertakings must cooperate and sacrifice private interests. The future is bright and limitless. We must take Russia, the United States, and Japan as models and unite absolutely and consistently against foreign countries." Labor Dispute at Wuhe Mercerizing Factory Resolved

Both Parties Sign Three Measures; Will Report to the Social Affairs Bureau to Close the Case 109

According to Dagong News Agency, the Wuhe Mercerizing and Dyeing Factory at the intersection of Yaozhu Church Road, Xujiahui, dismissed eleven workers, including Tang Fenglin, in July of this year, causing a dispute that has not been resolved after repeated mediation by Party and government agencies according to law. The Social Affairs Bureau summoned [the parties] for questioning the other day, instructing both parties to go out and resolve the dispute amicably. Two measures have been signed and announced to be resolved.

Announcement of Closure: After the labor party submitted a request to the Social Affairs Bureau for mediation, and because the manager of the factory, Zhang Shaoshan, was detained in the case, the shareholders declared the closure of the factory because there was no way to operate and the original capital had been almost exhausted, and reported to the Party and government agencies for record. The Mercerizing and Dyeing Workers' Union believed that the factory's sudden closure concerned the livelihood of the workers, and also reported to the Social Affairs Bureau, requesting [the bureau] to stop it. On the 8th of this month, the bureau summoned [the parties] for questioning based on the request of both labor and management. The person in charge, Tan Peiyan, advised both parties to compromise and try to resolve the dispute amicably outside. At 10 am yesterday, the factory side designated a shareholder, Niu Shanqing, to meet with Liu Jintai, the executive director of the union, to discuss three measures to resolve the dispute, formally signed [them], and then jointly reported to the Party and government agencies to close the case.

Measures for Resolution: The three measures for resolution signed by both parties yesterday are as follows: (1) The factory side will give each worker a subsidy of 50 yuan; (2) The union will repay 250 yuan for the expenses incurred by the union during the dispute over the dismissal of workers such as Tang Fenglin; (3) When the old shareholders resume business, they must still recruit 15 original member workers. If the factory is sold and opened by non-shareholders, they must do their best to introduce the work, etc.

Reason for Failure to Compare and Measure Rice Yesterday

Association Plans to Use Scales 111

The rice measures used by the rice industries in the North and South Cities have always used sea measures. The Social Affairs Bureau believes that this old-fashioned measure is no longer applicable and ordered the use of new measuring instruments. The Bean and Rice Public Association manufactured more than 500 [new instruments]. It was originally scheduled to be implemented in February of this year, and the old sea measures were abolished. It was reported to the Social Affairs Bureau for record. However, after the Shanghai war, the business of each industry was suspended, and the association requested several times to postpone the implementation. It has now been agreed that the new measuring instruments will be used uniformly in the North and South Cities on February 6 of next year. After the comparison is accurate, the various industries will be notified to prepare. Unexpectedly, the South City Measure Department and the boatmen had a dispute over the weight of the rice. Therefore, the association changed to using scales to avoid disputes between the Measure Department and the boatmen over the weight of the rice. The association originally scheduled to hold the winter rice comparison yesterday, so it was stopped.

Asia Petroleum's Tugboat KanSi Hits and Sinks a Stone Boat

Association Reports to Customs, Ordering Compensation 112

Zhang Hexing Sand and Stone Transport Lighter Company's No. 8247 lighter, carrying 40 tons of Songjiang stones, set sail for Shanghai on the 6th of this month. At about 6 pm, while traveling near Jiulimiao, Minhang, the Asia Petroleum Company's tugboat KanSi, towing two iron lighters, sailed out of Shanghai, also passing through the area. It was traveling at full speed and did not pull back the whistle, violently hitting the stern of the stone boat. Cattle Industry Association Calls for Lifting of Cattle Ban

Cattle for Plowing Distinguished from Old Cattle: Request for Inspection and Separate Lifting of Prohibition 113

The Shanghai Cattle and Sheep Trade Association, concerned about the excessive restrictions on cattle, harming both merchants and farmers, has issued a declaration to fellow tradesmen in various regions stating that since the Jiangsu Province floods last year, authorities, in order to protect agricultural affairs, issued an order prohibiting the export of plowing cattle, with a limit of eight months, from October of last year to the end of May this year, the term is now expired. Due to the January 28th Incident, the Jiangsu Province War Zone Relief Committee again sent a letter to the provincial government to continue the ban. This is the origin and process of the ban on plowing cattle. However, the ban has been prolonged year after year without a definite end date. Tens of thousands of our fellow tradesmen have lost their livelihood due to the ban. The long-term suspension of slaughter and transportation has caused direct and indirect harm to all. The suffering is especially severe for farmers who cannot dispose of their old cattle. It is found that cattle are divided into plowing cattle and old cattle. The ban should have a definite distinction. Cattle with two to four teeth are in their prime and suitable for operation and belong to plowing cattle. Cattle with six to eight teeth are in their declining years and are therefore old cattle. This identification is recorded in past official gazettes and publicly recognized by farmers and there is no need to avoid mentioning this. If all types are banned indiscriminately, the farmers' old cattle cannot be disposed of due to the ban and they will inevitably be left to die. Protecting agriculture will actually harm agriculture. Our association has repeatedly appealed to the authorities, requesting a separate lifting of the ban. Subsequently, we received a letter from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce approving the War Zone Relief Committee's telegram No. 45, which stated that the Shanghai Cattle and Sheep Trade Association's proposal to identify the age of cattle teeth to determine whether to ban transportation has been sent to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for joint handling. In accordance with this approval we have recorded the telegram and sent it to you. It is very clear that the age of the cattle should be the basis for identification. Last month, we received a comment from the Ministry of Industry stating that plowing cattle are of great importance to national agriculture and that a comprehensive plan is being formulated to establish appropriate measures. Before the Ministry issues a clear order, the original ban will remain in effect. It seems that the authorities' lifting of the ban is still far off. Since the ban, it has been observed that colluding local thugs and corrupt police openly and brazenly engage in private transportation, which has become increasingly rampant. Evidence from the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau's cattle inspection reports show little difference from before the ban. It only benefits a small number of private vendors and harms the majority of our fellow tradesmen. Therefore, as long as the ban is not lifted, farmers and merchants will continue to be restricted. In order to uphold the authorities' intention to protect agriculture and to alleviate the crisis for our fellow tradesmen, our association finds it necessary to request an inspection to distinguish plowing cattle from old cattle and lift the ban separately. We will therefore contact fellow tradesmen in various regions to request the authorities to devise a rescue plan, hoping that we will all work together to appeal and urge the authorities to consider the plight of the people of Jiangsu. This would not only be the good fortune of tens of thousands of endangered fellow tradesmen in Jiangsu Province, but also the great hope of farmers. This declaration is hereby made.

Reader Advisor

Discussion Results of Ms. Zhang Yunqiu's Questions 116

Ms. Zhang Yunqiu originally raised the questions: 1. Why does the boiling point of love for countless couples drop to zero? 2. What methods can be used to remedy such a tragedy?

Summary of the discussion: We believe that the questions raised by Ms. Zhang are actually a social problem closely related to the current social system. Before the entire social system is reformed and the entire social problem is resolved, this kind of local problem cannot be completely resolved. Even if it can, it is only a "treating the foot when it hurts" or "treating the head when it aches" approach. Even if the medicine you prescribe can accidentally heal one foot or one head, it is not enough to prove that the medicine you prescribe is a miraculous cure for all feet and all heads.

What exactly is the reason why the love of a couple drops from boiling point to freezing point? Many letters reply that it is because men are fond of the new and tired of the old, because they fail to understand the true meaning of love, because of the oppression of married life, because women are economically dependent, because the two parties fail to understand each other deeply. Some people also use the analogy of "too much honey is not sweet" and "the spring of a clock loosens after running for a long time," believing that the relaxation of marital love is inevitable and natural. The various opinions mentioned above are of course all very correct, but they do not grasp the core of the problem and do not find the real root cause. What is said above is only the "fruit," and we should further investigate the source of those "fruits."

Perhaps some people disagree with this opinion! Then I must ask: Why are women economically dependent? Why should a certain group of people feel the oppression of life? Why are men allowed to be fond of the new and tired of the old? If you do not find a root cause, then can you correctly answer these questions except by using something like "the theory of destiny" or "extreme idealism" to explain them tyrannically?

···········································

Since the establishment of the system of private property and men became the center of society, women have been transformed from "free people" to disguised slaves, disguised property. She is only a man's "wife," not a "social person." In other words, she is "a man's," not "society's." She has no freedom, no will. She cannot stand on an equal footing with men. Her daily life and diet all depend on men. Therefore, men can "cherish the new and abandon the old," can "think of moving" when they see "difference," and can use their own likes and dislikes to determine the fate of women. || If we want to explain the first problem psychologically, we should base it on this observation to understand and distinguish it.

Secondly, if we say that the decline of a couple's feelings is due to "the compulsion of life," it is especially clear that this fact is intimately linked to the social system. If everyone in this society works and everyone has food to eat, as in the final stage of Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People society, then there would be no fact that some people alone feel the compulsion of life, and there would be no tragedy between husband and wife caused by this. Therefore, to explain this problem from this point of view, we should especially correctly grasp the concept.

However, we are ultimately people in a real society. The reform of society is not something that can be realized in a moment, so we cannot but do our best to remedy the tragedies before us. Even if we treat the head when it aches and treat the foot when it hurts, it is not a happy thing if we can accidentally heal one foot or one head.

Here, we summarize the opinions of more than 300 letters and create a remedy plan as follows:

1. Before marriage, the two parties must understand each other deeply; 2. The two parties should be based on reason and should not be purely emotional; 3. The two parties must respect each other's personality and should not take a playful attitude; 4. The two parties should seek economic independence and be thrifty; 5. The two parties should pay attention to physiological health; 6. The two parties should forgive each other and often recall past love; 7. If possible, small separations should be made frequently; 8. If absolutely incompatible, divorce should be implemented.

Small Knotted Hat and Red Paper Package as Identification

Detectives Went as Agreed and Arrested Two People

They agreed to meet at around 2:00 pm this afternoon near the Yingji Hotel at the corner of Guangdong Road and Fujian Road. The person coming must wear a small knotted hat and hold a red paper package as a sign, otherwise, they will use drastic measures to set his house on fire. He had never met the two defendants. According to Cen Rukai, the plaintiff is his brother-in-law. The second time, he went to Fujian Road with the Chinese and foreign detectives from the police station and waited near the entrance of the Yingji Hotel. At that time, Liu said that he could introduce him to a place to be a rickshaw driver, and then asked him to go to Fujian Road to pick up a loan. The person wearing a small knotted melon-skin hat and holding a red paper package was the one. He didn't need to be afraid. If the money was obtained, they would each receive 20 yuan as a reward. He heard that the name of the lender was Ah Hong, who was a friend of Liu and lived in a hotel. He knew nothing about the threatening letters or who delivered them. Liu Ruiyan confessed that he knew Ah Hong and that Ah Hong asked him to go to pick up the money and gave him 20 yuan as a reward. At that time, he did not ask Huang's representative to go to the Great World, etc. Hua Detective Mao of the police station stated that the investigation in this case revealed that Ah Hong and two others, who are at large, initiated the plan in advance and opened room number 12 at the Xingaosheng Hotel at No. 178 Guangdong Road. From October 10th to the date of the incident on October 22nd, they went out together and did not return. When the two defendants were arrested, the second defendant, Liu Ruiyan, said to the representative Cen Rukai, "There may be detectives here, let's go to the Great World." He heard it clearly. Assessor Zhao verified the confessions, designated a lawyer to provide free defense for the two defendants, and then sent them back to detention. A date was set for the verdict.

Prevention and Emergency Treatment for Coal Gas Poisoning 120

The Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau issued a public notice yesterday, saying, "Citizens, the weather is getting cold and everyone wants to install stoves for heating. Do you still remember the tragedies of people dying from coal gas poisoning in the past? In the past, such tragedies often occurred in places like Beiping. Later, with experience, people knew the prevention and emergency treatment methods. This harm has been reduced a lot. The bureau is now specially explaining it to everyone. 1. Causes of poisoning: When coal balls or coal lumps have not been burned to the extremely flourishing stage, they emit a gas called carbon monoxide. This gas is colorless and odorless, and it is often not easy to detect. If you smell it too much, breathing will become tight, your face will turn red, you will become dizzy, and your mind will become unclear as if you were drunk. If the poisoning is too deep, you will lose your life. Even if it is mild, you will be sick for a few days. 2. Prevention methods: When burning coal or charcoal in a room, be sure to install a chimney or vent pipe. If there is no chimney pipe or vent pipe, you must burn it to the extremely flourishing stage in a place with sufficient outdoor air before moving it indoors. The same should be done when adding coal. Also, when burning coal in the room, you must open one or two of the windows and doors along the empty space to allow the air in the room to circulate and exchange with the outdoor air. It is best not to burn coal or other things while sleeping at night. If you are still burning them, the doors and windows should not be closed tightly and be airtight. In short, when burning things in the room, you must ensure that the outdoor air and the indoor air can circulate and exchange sufficiently. People in the room should also often go outdoors to relax. 3. Emergency treatment for poisoning: If someone is unfortunately poisoned by coal gas, quickly move him to a place with very smooth air, loosen his clothes, and perform artificial respiration. The method is as follows: Loosen the clothes of the poisoned person, make him lie flat, and use pillows or other things to elevate his back to allow his lungs to open. Stand behind his head, slowly lift the poisoned person's arms from the front, extend them over his head, and then slowly lower them to both sides of his body and gently press them flat. Repeat this until the poisoned person wakes up. After waking up, you still need to seek medical treatment to restore your health. Otherwise, the root of the disease will be lurking, and you must be careful. It is best to seek emergency treatment while quickly asking a Western doctor to diagnose. The above is very common knowledge. Because some people still do not understand, there are often tragic news of people dying from coal gas poisoning. With this notice, I hope everyone will pay attention at all times and not be careless. This is a special notice.

Shanghai South Winter Relief First Institute 121

Has Already Begun Receiving

The Shanghai Charity Group Zihui Office's Shanghai South Winter Relief Institute first took in the first batch at the Chaozhou Guild Hall at the South Railway Station yesterday. Wu Xingsheng Died from Electric Shock Fall 123

Wu Xingsheng, a local, 21 years old, was a plasterer. A few days ago, he was working at a height of about 30 feet in the China Aluminum Products Factory at No. 1550 Meizhou Road, Hudong. At 10:30 am, he accidentally touched a power line and fell down, suffering severe head injuries. The factory reported to the Yangshupu Police Station, which ordered Detective Liu to investigate. He was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but he died shortly after. The body was taken to the Pei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday, Prosecutor Guo, appointed by the First Special District Court, and forensic scribe Wang Zuxing, etc., arrived at the morgue to examine the body and investigate the case. According to Yao Genzong's statement, he was a plasterer and was working in the same place as the deceased that day. He climbed to a high place first. At that time, the power switch had not been turned on, so although he touched the power line, he did not get an electric shock. However, the deceased was climbing up when the power switch was suddenly turned on, causing him to be electrocuted and fall down. The power switch was turned on by Liu Shaofu in the factory. He did not know that Yao and the deceased were working at the time, which caused the accident. After obtaining the confession, Prosecutor Guo ordered that the body of the deceased Wu Xingsheng, male, was indeed injured in the head before death. The body was handed over to his father, Wu Shengsong, to take back for burial.

Sedan Smashes into Truck 126

Six Laborers Injured

The Xinhe Xing Auto Repair Company at 170 Gongping Road, near the Heng Road intersection, was repairing an Austin truck, license number 16524, belonging to the Xinglong Auto Shop of Xia Hai Temple. The repairs were completed. Yesterday at around 9:00 PM, the driver Li Changming was driving the truck with nine laborers heading from Gongping Road towards Des Vie Road. When the truck reached the corner of North Sichuan Road and Qiujiang Road, a black sedan, license number 2972, suddenly emerged from a side road and struck the side of the truck, causing the Austin to overturn. Six laborers on board were injured: Wu Lingen, a 14-year-old from Tongzhou, suffered a fractured left arm; Lu Youdao, 19, injured his neck; Chen Shisheng, 28, injured his back; Xu Aqing, 16, injured his right arm; Qian Xingtang, 31, injured his buttocks; and Wu Fuchang, 29, injured his left leg. All were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Inspection Report of the China Land Reclamation Bank 127

The China Land Reclamation Bank issued an inspection report on its reserve for note issuance. The report stated that the bank's issuing vault and operating vault have always been completely separated. According to the bank's articles of association, the cash reserve should be above 70% and the guarantee reserve should be below 30%. On the 10th of this month, after an inspection by accountant Wang Zikang, along with Xu Jiqing and Xu Busun representing the board of directors and supervisors, the results were as follows: The total amount of exchange notes issued was 5,183,000 silver dollars. The total amount of the exchange note reserve was 5,183,000 silver dollars, including: Cash reserve of 4,184,388 silver dollars, and a guarantee reserve of 998,612 silver dollars. The cash reserve accounts for slightly more than 80%, while the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly less than 20%. This report is hereby issued.

The Wenzhou-Chuzhou Salt Affairs Improvement Association sent a telegram to the chambers of commerce of the Yongjia and the Liang counties of the Wenzhou-Chuzhou areas, saying: Each chamber of commerce forwarded to each group is aware that the salt tax contractors in Wenzhou-Chuzhou have been disrupting for many years. The people of the Association have seen the evils with their own eyes and dare not remain silent. We have collected evidence to sue and deployed to eliminate the fierce and protect the people. In recent months, such as controlling the removal of the Inspector-General Bureau and canceling the contractor system, recovering excess charges, and banning unlicensed transportation, all have been realized. In the case of no fraud, the court recently announced the sentence of detention and fines. The Association's proposal of 19 have been fulfilled. Although this is due to the court's clear investigation and judgment, the Yongjia Salt Affairs Improvement Association's efforts and struggles have contributed greatly to this success. Now, at the beginning of the rectification, old habits still exist. The most important thing to pay attention to is the revision of the salt tax regulations in the two counties. The deployment has been decided and promulgated, and all fees set by the contractors have been abolished. However, it is feared that those in remote rural areas may not be well-informed and that the villagers may be easily deceived. Therefore, we specifically state the total amount of the total number of regulated tax: The Taizhou in Chuzhou, the Jin Yongwu salts and the soy sauce salts in Wenzhou are all set at 4.1 yuan. Yueqing Yuhuan light tax is set at $1.20. is set at 1 yuan for salt, All surtaxes are already included. There are no other donations or fees. We hope to spread this information widely so that everyone is aware. If there are contractors whose poisons have not been eliminated or any events that should be innovated, we dare to hope that you will clearly inform us by letter. The Association will naturally file a complaint and deploy to complete the improvement, so that the people of the two counties can receive practical benefits. Letter to the Editor 139

To the Editor: Regarding your newspaper's report on November 26th that our company privately installed wireless telephone equipment for direct communication with Hong Kong, Macau, Guangzhou, etc., which impairs China's telecommunications sovereignty, this is inconsistent with the facts. Our company entered into a contract with the Macau government on October 29th, agreeing that our company would supply and install a 500-watt broadcasting station. There was no agreement or intention for international wireless telephone communication. Our company is only engaged in the manufacture and sale of machinery. We have no intention of privately establishing wireless telephone stations with Shanghai, Guangzhou, or any part of the Ministry of Communications. How can this impair China's telecommunications sovereignty? In addition to sending a special letter to the International Telecommunications Bureau and the Ministry of Communications, we are writing to your newspaper to clarify this. We hope you will make a correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Asia Electric Company, December 9th.
