Important News: Jiangsu Education Commissioner Zhou Fo Hai Inspects Northern Jiangsu (6) 140

Braving Wind and Rain to Rugao

Whole City Warmly Welcomes

The situation of Jiangsu Education Commissioner Zhou Fohai's inspection in Nantong and his trip to Shanghai and Beijing was reported yesterday. Now, we supplement the record of Zhou's situation in Rugao. On the morning of the 5th, at 8:00 AM, he attended the anniversary week of the Provincial Tongzhong School and gave an extremely sincere speech to the students. The general idea was that provincial schools are the focus of attention for county, public, and private schools, so expectations are high and supervision is strict. He was very pleased that the students of Tongzhong were able to strive in their studies, but there were two points to note: first, pay attention to physical education; second, strictly observe order. Normal school students will be future teachers and should pay attention to this. Teachers and staff should train students with a strict approach, otherwise both teachers and students will regret it later. In the afternoon of the same day, at 2:00 PM, braving wind and rain, he took a car to Rugao. He arrived in Rugao at 5:00 PM. County Magistrate Qian, representatives of the county party headquarters, standing committee members, Director of Education Bureau Sha, the three directors of the Finance, Construction, and Public Security Bureaus, and representatives of various agencies and organizations were all waiting at the station to welcome him. High-hanging welcome banners were displayed at the station. Zhou got out of the car amidst the sounds of military music and met with the welcomers one by one. Then, he switched to a rickshaw and went to Guangxu Building to rest. All the shops along the way hung flags to express their warm welcome. Welcome slogans were posted all over the streets and alleys. After a short rest, Zhou immediately led Section Chiefs Chen and Xiang, Supervisor Cao, Director Yi, and others to the Provincial Rugao Normal School to inspect self-study. He examined the students one by one in detail and inquired about the daily teaching of the staff and the actual situation of students' extracurricular activities. On the morning of the 6th, he went to Rugao Normal School again to inspect teaching and gave serious criticisms and guidance. Representatives of the Rugao Education Association came to visit. Zhou gave a comprehensive and concise instruction on local education. Then, he went to inspect the affiliated primary school of Rugao Normal School. He gave detailed instructions on the staffing of the school. Then, he went to inspect the County Experimental Elementary School. The school's children were full of "Welcome Education Commissioner Zhou" slogans, which were colorful and dazzling. Children took off their hats to salute Zhou, one after another, full of innocent and unrestrained air. Afterwards, he went to inspect the County People's Education Center for a week. By then it was noon, so he returned to his residence for lunch. At 1:00 PM in the afternoon, he went to the Wu Xiang Primary School, the Chen Jia Xiang Primary School, and the Ji Feng Elementary School to inspect them in detail. At 4:00 PM, he went to the County Public Association and the library. At 5:00 PM, he went to the Education Bureau to review work diaries and all records, paying particular attention to the county's finances. He also instructed Section Chiefs Chen and Xiang to convene a discussion with the supervisors and education committee members. Section Chief Xiang also inspected the classes of the People's School attached to the People's Education Center. He returned to his residence at 9:00 PM.

Junior High School Curriculum Standards (2) 141

Physical Education 142

First. Objectives

(1) To strengthen physical fitness, so that the body and mind develop healthily, in preparation for revitalizing the nation.

(2) To cultivate obedience, hard work, autonomy, loyalty, courage, cooperation, discipline, and other civic virtues through group sports.

(3) To develop the sports skills needed in life.

(4) To improve the agility of physical reactions.

(5) To develop graceful and correct posture.

(6) To develop the habit of using sports as entertainment.

Second. Time Allocation

(1) Regular classes: three hours per week.

(2) Morning exercises: ten minutes every morning.

(3) Extracurricular activities: at least half an hour every day.

Third. Teaching Material Outline

(1) First Year

(a) Games, (b) Skillful Exercises, (c) Lively Apparatus Exercises (for winter), (d) Ball Sports, (e) Track and Field Sports, (f) National Martial Arts, (g) Dance (reduced for boys), (h) Natural Activities, including swimming, waterskiing, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others, used as much as possible in extracurricular time, (i) Corrective Exercises, selected by students with physical defects, (j) Basic Exercises, adopting the basic movements of ball sports, track and field sports, and apparatus exercises, taught in a natural way, (k) Gentle Exercises (selected by those who are not suitable for strenuous exercise).

(2) Second Year

(a) Games, (b) Skillful Exercises, (c) Group Mixed Continuous Apparatus Exercises, (d) Ball Sports, (e) Track and Field Sports (reduced for girls), (f) National Martial Arts, (g) Dance (reduced for boys), (h) Natural Activities, including swimming, ice skating, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others, used as much as possible in extracurricular time, (i) Corrective Exercises, selected by students with physical defects, (j) Natural Gymnastics, (k) Gentle Exercises (selected by those who are not suitable for strenuous exercise).

(3) Third Year

(a) Games, (b) Skillful Exercises, (c) Lively Apparatus Exercises, (d) Ball Sports, (e) Track and Field Sports (reduced for girls), (f) National Martial Arts, (g) Dance (reduced for boys), (h) Natural Activities, including swimming, ice skating, mountain climbing, riding, rowing, and others, used as much as possible in extracurricular time, (i) Corrective Exercises, selected by students with physical defects, (j) Natural Gymnastics, (k) Gentle Exercises (selected by those who are not suitable for strenuous exercise).

Fourth. Summary of Implementation Methods

(1) Assignments

(a) Regular classes, (b) Morning exercises, (c) Extracurricular activities, (d) Organization of various extracurricular activities, (A) Intra-school competitions, (B) Inter-school competitions, (C) Excursions and trips, (D) Various designs and performances.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points

(a) Apply the overall learning method and analytical learning method of ordinary teaching methods, and the law of preparation, law of practice, and law of effect of educational psychology.

(b) Regular classes, morning exercises, and extracurricular activities should be interconnected to avoid repetition, so as not to make students bored. (A) Regular class content emphasizes basic training and teaching methods and rules. The teacher's workload is heavier. (B) Extracurricular activities emphasize the students' actual practice. The teacher is only responsible for management. (C) Morning exercises or activities between classes pay attention to the harmonious activities of the body. Their role is to regulate life and focus on natural movements.

(c) Use group competition methods as much as possible.

(d) Hold skill tests at least once per semester. At the beginning of the semester, announce the test method in advance to encourage students to work hard in practice.

(e) National martial arts should start from strengthening physical fitness. The posture should be correct, the movements should be lively, and the meaning and function of each movement must be understood.

(f) Schools without indoor sports facilities should make full use of ordinary indoor equipment for special sports activities.

(g) Sanitary facilities such as bathrooms should be fully equipped.

(h) Use holidays to create large-scale sports design activities, such as celebrations and joint sports meetings.

(i) Unite with other groups in sports to compare and promote progress.

(j) Use ability grouping methods as much as possible. Physical education grading cannot be based on ordinary intelligence grading. Because the age of students varies from place to place and the degree of physical development is different, students of the same grade may not be suitable for the same type of teaching materials. Therefore, within the possible scope, ability grading should be used as much as possible. The grading method should be based on the following six standards (see Appendix)

(k) Conduct health checkups at the beginning of each school year.

(l) Natural Gymnastics.

(m) When teaching various sports, if it is not possible to apply the overall learning method, or the posture is incorrect, basic exercises can be used to practice the basic methods of each sport.

Fifth. Appendix: Grading Method

(1) Gender, (2) Results of physical examination, (3) Age, height, weight, (4) Physical fitness, (5) Skills, (6) Grade.

Now, the six grading methods are briefly explained below.

(1) Gender: Boys and girls gradually develop differently after the age of twelve or thirteen.

Interests are also different, so physical education above junior high school should be taught completely in separate classes.

(2) Results of Health Examination: Health examination is one of the most important items in school administration. At least every student should be examined once a year. The results of the examination should be used as a reference for physical education grading. Students with poor physical development or defects should be given special instruction.

(3) Age, Height, Weight: It is difficult to teach students of different ages and development together in physical education class. Many schools use age, height, and weight grading methods. Some use only one, some use two together, and some use three together, and using three together is the best. McCloy's Physical Skills Standards Score Table can be borrowed and applied. A simple method is attached below. It can still be changed during application. For example, the table is divided into seven levels. We can divide it into two or three levels according to the index obtained by the actual junior high school students.

Unrecovered From Illness, Fear of Delaying Bureau Affairs 143

National Compilation and Translation Bureau Publishes "The Improvement of Chinese Education" 147

"The Reconstruction of Chinese Education" is a report of the investigation of Chinese education by the International League of Nations Educational Survey Team. It is now compiled and published by the National Compilation and Translation Bureau. The content is divided into the situation of Chinese education, national education and external influences, teaching spirit, administrative principles, teachers and staff, primary education, teacher training, secondary education, university education, adult education, etc., all of which have appropriate reports and criticisms, and suggestions for improvement, but without attached preliminary reform plans. The so-called "onlookers see more of the game," and the stone from another mountain can be used to polish jade. It is truly a necessary reference book for domestic education administrators and teachers at all levels.

Sports

Yesterday's Two Scota Cup Games Ended Displeasantly 162

A Misfortune for the Football Community

In the second week of the Scota Cup, the Yu You team faced the Lancashire team in a match at the baseball field yesterday. Yu You had a very good situation and seemed to have hope of winning. Unexpectedly, after winning two consecutive goals, they actually scored two goals themselves. Later, Lancashire scored another goal, and the score became two to three, with Yu You in a subordinate position. Of course, it was not difficult to reverse the defeat, but in the second half, because the referee's law enforcement was not strict, the players' actions were unchecked, and Yu You repeatedly made things difficult for the referee, and even expressed the attitude of not continuing the game. The game was temporarily suspended for two or three minutes. With the utmost persuasion of Chen Shaojun, the players continued the game. It is not known that when the final game had only six or seven minutes left, Yu You could not maintain its short time and ended in disorder. The referee also had no way to do so. Whether the result is valid will have to be resolved by the Western Football Association.

Winning Two Goals First But Sending Two Goals Oneself 163

The bell rang three times, and Yu You kicked off first, and the momentum was extremely strong. Within twenty-five minutes, Wang Zhangbao won two consecutive goals, and for a time, they were overjoyed and felt that their spirits had doubled. But Lancashire was calm and unhurried, and worked hard to counterattack, so Yu You's goal was dangerous, and they often showed signs of panic and disorder. Liang Gongxun first treated the guests, scoring a goal himself. Coincidentally, it can be said that there is no coincidence. In a short time, Yu You Zhu scored a goal in front of the goal, the ball slipped backwards and hit Dong Xiaopei's head again, and rolled into his own goal. Ah Liang was unprepared and lost another goal, so Yu You's vitality was greatly damaged and felt regretful.

Losing Another Goal, Yu You's Life is Injured 164

After the result of the first half was two to two, not long after the second half started, Lancashire's right winger Kai Zhi scored another goal, making it three to two, and Yu You turned defeat into victory. From then on, the situation of the game was unsightly. Unexpectedly, Yu You expressed unwillingness to continue the game, leaving a stain on the senior team.

Loose Refereeing is the Root Cause 165

Yesterday's game had more barbarous player movements than the previous Jinan and Donghua games. Yu You's disorderly ending was also unexpected. However, the root cause is that the referee's law enforcement was not strict. In this situation, if the judgment is strict and the law is enforced like a mountain, and no relaxation is allowed, then the players will not be able to kick people without kicking the ball, and the event of leaving the field halfway will not occur. As for the team, it should adhere to the rule of "I will not offend others unless they offend me," and should be tolerant and generous, and eliminate vanity, then unfortunate events can be avoided. Chinese teams have repeatedly given foreigners a bad impression. What a sigh!

Impolite Spectators are Also One Reason 166

Recently, in the stadium, there are often a small number of bad spectators who yell and cheer, contributing to the unprecedented stadium and creating the possibility of unruliness. Yesterday's Yu You incident was partly caused by a small number of bad spectators who helped Yu You leave the field. With only six or seven minutes left in the game, the audience even asked the Xie Jin Association to refund the tickets, making unreasonable demands. This is even more evident here. It is hoped that enthusiastic spectators and Chinese team players will never act on impulse. They must always think about the skills of the game, perform fewer deviant actions, avoid being ridiculed by foreigners, degrading their personality, and insulting the national prestige.

First Half Win of Two to One Results in Failure of Three to Four

It is truly fortunate that Jinan, in an incomplete state, was able to defeat Lacks, which possesses both a strong offense and defense, in yesterday's Western League competition. The result was 4-3, with referee Bolt officiating.

Jiang Shanjing is Intelligent and Brave

The Meaning of Scoring One Goal is Unknown 182

People say that Jiang Shanjing is brave, but it is a pity that he is prone to over-the-top fouls. However, in recent matches, he has shown great improvement, being as fast as a swallow and as steady as Mount Tai. With Gu Shangrang's assistance yesterday, he was able to handle the situation with ease. At the beginning of the match, Jinan's morale was shaken by the absence of its mainstay, Xu Yahui. The opponent took advantage of this weakness and launched a major offensive. At that time, enemy figures frequently appeared in front of Jinan's goal. Although Jiang and Gu did their best to resist, their efforts were commendable. However, Lacks' poor shooting also made it difficult to win. Suddenly, Liu Zukan lofted a shot towards the goal, and the forwards surged forward like a tide. The opponent's inner defenders also rushed to defend. The ball appeared

Strange, leaping into the net from between the feet of both sides. Both sides were stunned and did not know what it meant. Jinan's victory in this goal seemed to be a harbinger of their victory that day.

Fan Enshi's Skills are Amazing

Two Long Shots Score Consecutively 183

The Lacks team has discovered a new player named Fan Shi, who appeared in the Hong Kong and Shanghai competitions a few years ago. He currently holds an important position in the team's midfield. Observing his superb skills, he will surely be able to replace Ga Xu's position in the future. At that time, seeing that Jinan's inner defenses were difficult to break and the goalkeeper was easy to deceive, he switched to long-range shooting. Once, from 50 yards away, he shot directly into the upper goalpost. Another time, from over 40 yards away, he also scored from the left corner. If Xie Quanhe had been prepared earlier, he could have prevented the disaster, but he was unable to react in time. In the first half, they lost 1-2.

Mei Hongbao is Small in Stature but Fast on his Feet

Achieves a Draw Within Five Minutes 184

Jinan's center forward, Luo Haiguang, has had mediocre results recently, but in the five minutes after the start of the second half, he relied on his courage to score a goal. He took it in and attacked, but seeing the enemy's reinforcements arriving, he quickly used his ingenuity to transfer it to the right. Mei Hongbao was prepared, sprinted to catch up, and with his foot, the ball went out like an arrow straight into the goal, creating a 2-2 draw. Afterwards, Jinan's momentum was fierce, greatly different from before. Lacks' goal was full of trouble from then on. The goalkeeper was frightened and nearly lost the lead. Once, Jiang Shanjing kicked a free kick, imitating Fan Enshi, going straight for the goal, but it rebounded off the post. Mei then headed the ball out of bounds. With many twists and turns, Pei Ke suddenly broke through from the left and crossed the ball into the goal. Lacks took the lead again with a score of 3-2.

Chen Zhenhe is Strong and Unstoppable

Scores Two More Goals to Maintain the Victory 185

Chen Zhenhe is one of the famous generals of Shanghai. Recently, many have found it difficult to deal with his partner. In fact, he has had no place to use his skills. Yesterday, because he was being watched, he switched to alternating with Liu. The opponent lost their defense, and Chen was able to break through from the left. When he reached a critical point, he hooked the ball with his foot, and it landed in front of the goal. Mei headed the ball into the goal, making the score 3-3. Gu Haiguang committed a foul and was sent off the field. Jinan still continued to advance ferociously. Mei Hong displayed his skills and picked the ball up, and it happened to be in front of the goal. Chen Zhenhe took advantage of the situation to shoot, as if to compensate Gu, and surprisingly, they turned defeat into victory with a score of 4-3. With ten minutes remaining, the entire Jinan army retreated to focus on defense, not making any rash moves, fearing that they would suffer unexpected setbacks. Thus, they were able to maintain their victory and return triumphantly.

The Jiangzhe Private Nine Middle School Football and Basketball Tournament, which began yesterday at Yuelun University in Fanwangdu, Shanghai, has reached its climax after two days of competition. Huilan will meet Jinling in the final.

John Wins Taowu Eight to Zero. In the other group of the consolation group semi-final, John played against Taowu. John was quite strong, and unfortunately lost to Huilan 2-3 in the preliminary round. Hopes for the Championship are Dampened 190

Xiaguang Wins Jiangwan Qingguang Wins Ye Shi

The Hujiang basketball team, in this Western Youth Basketball League, had great ambition to defeat the Navy and seize the championship. However, if they can defeat the Navy and remain undefeated in the future, there is still hope. In the other three Group A matches, Chizhi defeated the US Navy 40-21, Xiaguang defeated Jiangwan 43-27, and Qingguang defeated Ye Shi 63-31. Hujiang Suffered a Miserable Defeat

Nanxing Has Made Great Progress 191

Nanxing's victory over Hujiang was certainly not accidental. Last night's performance showed that they have made significant progress. Their movements were swift, and their defense was tight, preventing Hujiang's forwards from using their skills despite their bravery. Their attacks were well-organized, calm, and unhurried, which was the reason for their victory.

Hujiang's Fatal Wound 192

Hujiang's defeat was due to a lackluster performance, which cannot be denied. Because their defense was not tight, Nanxing was able to break through at times. The forwards were also shaken by this. Although Wu Guolin remained the same as before, Feng Nianhua also missed shots. The biggest fatal wound was that their general, Qian Jingyong, was sent off for four fouls in less than ten minutes of the first half. The team was greatly shaken, and Wu Guolin's solitary struggle could not save the overall situation.

Nanxing Rises Suddenly 193

Although the initial battle was fierce, Hujiang still held the advantage, leading 7-5. After Liu Shenzhan's two-point free throw, Nanxing suddenly rose to 10-7. At 14-8, Hujiang's Qian Jingyong was sent off, and Nanxing's momentum became even stronger. In the first half, Nanxing led by as many as eight points with a score of 18-10.

Both Sides Engage in Close Combat 194

At the start of the second half, Hujiang, with Wu Guolin's two long shots, quickly narrowed the score, with the score becoming 17-18, only one point behind. Continuing their efforts, Hujiang attacked desperately, and the score fluctuated up and down by one point, with the entire stadium being tense. However, Hujiang's Feng Nianhua was restricted by three fouls, making the outcome uncertain, and everyone was sweating for Hujiang.

The Last Five Minutes 195

With five minutes remaining, Hujiang, with Wu Guolin's one point, took the lead by two points at 26-24. Nanxing's Bao Xindi then tied the game with a throw. With two minutes remaining, Nanxing took the lead by one point at 28-27. Sun Baoqing had a chance for a free throw, but missed both throws. Turning around, Sun committed his fourth foul and was sent off. Hujiang's situation was hopeless. At the final score, Nanxing won 30-27.

Commercial News: Financial Gold Market Shows Signs of Weakness

Weekly Fluctuations of Fourteen Taels, Strong Consolidation and a Drop of Four Taels 199

(With a fluctuation of five taels outside) Although the market trend yesterday was not overly volatile, there was also a fluctuation of more than five taels. Reviewing the initial weakness and subsequent stability, the final price was slightly lower by four qian compared to yesterday. Traders did not engage in much trading and their sentiment was hesitant. The initial decline was due to the impact of the recent decline and subsequent rise of the American bank, further indications, and the rebound in exchange rates. Subsequently, foreign exchange fluctuated slightly, with the British pound remaining stable and the American dollar easing, so the price of gold fluctuated slightly. Furthermore, there were reports in foreign news about the American debt situation, which was complex. Nevertheless, buyers on the surface once exceeded the 800-tael mark, but then weakened. The market was halted at 6 p.m. Checking the situation this week, it was chaotic, caused by conflicting war debt news. The highest price was 807 taels and 4 qian on Monday, and the price fluctuated greatly until it reached 787 taels and 8 qian on Thursday. It eventually stood at the 800-tael mark, with a total weekly fluctuation of 19 taels and 6 qian and a consolidated decrease of 4 taels, reversing the trend after four consecutive weeks of gains.

(A Slight Decline of Four Qian in Half a Day) The market opened at 797 taels and 2 qian in the morning, a decrease of 2 taels and 9 qian. There were then fluctuations of three to four qian. Dadecheng and other firms sold, immediately dropping by more than one tael to 95 taels and 6 qian. Suddenly, there was news that Citibank bought February American dollars at 4375 and also bought December at 25, and Hengxing entered the market to buy, and Fuyu and hedgers also bought, immediately rising by 1 tael and a half to 7 taels and 1 qian at 9:10 a.m. Huabi came out with March half-yuan, Zhaofeng, Changfeng, and retail investors sold, and immediately fell by more than 1 tael and 6-7 qian, ultimately reaching 5 taels and 4 qian. Huabi then absorbed February American dollars at 4375, and Dongya absorbed January at 3125. Furthermore, as the HSBC listing announcement had not been changed, it was 6 taels and 4 qian at 9:30 a.m. Subsequently, Hengxing, Hengyuantai, Yuanmao, Yongbingxing, Futai, Hongkangyong, etc. all competed to buy, but there was not much change in the exchange rate. The December American dollar settlement was at 25, and the old Citibank bought forward at 625 for March, hedging half-yuan, and the price of gold rose by more than one tael. However, from 9:30 a.m. to 10:30 a.m., there was only a few qian rebound, hovering between 97 and 8 taels. It was then heard that France seemed to be able to pay American debt, but other debts required that conditions be proposed and repaid. There was also news that England planned to borrow new money to repay old debts and was unwilling to use cash to repay, so traders were psychologically hesitant and the market price was slow to rise, but Zhifeng, Yongtianfeng, Yongyifeng, Yongyuanmao, etc. bought, because the bank had absorbed half a yuan for the March American dollar, and also bought English gold against the ninepence for January and 0625 for February. Until 11:00 a.m., the price of gold rose to 800 taels and 08 qian, and there was a brief drop of 1 tael. However, it hovered around 800 taels, and Yifeng, Yongda, Decheng, Yuantai, Wanxing, and retail investors sold, falling to 98 taels and 9 qian after 11:30 a.m. Yifeng, Fuyu, Dafeng, Hengheng Yu, etc. took advantage of this to buy, and Huabi Bank mutually traded February English gold for 9 pence in the near term and 8 pence 9375. Huabi absorbed half a yuan for the March American dollar, so the price rose by more than 1 tael, closing at 800 taels and 03 qian. At the noon close, it was 799 taels and 7 qian, a further decrease of 4 qian from the previous day, and it then traded at 9 taels and 12 qian. Securities and Bond Prices: First Down, Then Up 203

(Whole Six Bonds Dropped Sharply, Others Recovered Slightly, Trading Reached 12.5 Million)

Yesterday (the 10th), the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange had a good futures market. The market prices fluctuated greatly, and trading was active. The spot market continued to be extremely scarce. At the beginning of the morning, due to news of tense situation in the Northeast and the Japanese army invading Rehe, market sentiment was uneasy, and sellers surged. All prices continued the trend of the previous day and declined sharply. For example, the Disbandment Bond price once fell to around 53 yuan. Other prices also declined significantly. The market environment turned better in the later market, and the market had a turning point. Large investors had already started to buy, and retail buying was also better than before. All prices rose in unison. As a result, compared to the previous day, only the Whole Six current and futures contracts and the Customs Duty forward contracts fell sharply. The Reorganization Bond also decreased slightly, and the 20-Year Financial Short-Term Bond fell by 4 yuan and was suspended from trading. Other bonds recovered by about half a yuan. The bond market will shift according to changes in the diplomatic situation. It is said that the total spot trading for the day was only 5,000 yuan, and futures trading was more than 12.5 million yuan.

American Cotton Trading Restricted 206

Two Problems: War Debt and Relief Legislation

New York, 9th Telegram: A report on the cotton market for the week. Yesterday, the sudden increase in the government's cotton production estimate, reaching a huge 780,000, was unexpected. However, the impact on the market was minimal because prices had already fallen, and there were few speculative bulls. Therefore, when prices fell, sales from the South and bull liquidations were absorbed by colleagues buying and short covering. At the same time, the March contract reached the low price of June. However, due to the uncertainty of war debt and cotton field relief legislation, trading was restricted. Sources here are still questioning whether a fundamental relief plan will be passed in the current congressional agenda. At the same time, investor sentiment, based on original prices, seems to be still focused on the increase in harvest estimates, which may further strengthen their attack. If the war debt problem is resolved, trading may improve. The weekend statistics are attached on the left.

Areas for Improvement in Inexpensive Drying, Production, and Packaging of Lanzhu Branches 209

(Lychee Dried) Lanzhu branches are produced in Tongzhou, Fujian. This year, due to abundant harvests in Haikou, Guangdong, and other places, sales have been greatly affected. In previous years, market prices were comparable to those of Jinshan branches produced in Guangdong and even surpassed them occasionally. However, this year, market prices have suddenly reversed. The reason is that the selection of Lanzhu branches is not done properly. For example, in ordinary mixed-brand Lanzhu branches, small, pointed grains are mixed in up to 20%. After various firms purchase them, there are very few outlets for the original goods. Sorting them requires time and is not cost-effective. Therefore, even during periods of strong sales, almost no one cares about Lanzhu branches in the Shanghai market. However, Jinshan branches are quite active, with liquidation in various places. Even Hang and other inland areas, which have sales outlets, have switched to Jinshan branches. However, it is difficult to get a good price. From this, we can see that the reason for the stagnation of Lanzhu branches is entirely due to the impurity of the goods. The advantages and disadvantages of Lanzhu branches and Jinshan branches are described below so that the owners in the producing area can pay attention to them and avoid making mistakes.

(Jinshan Branches) "Packaging" Each box weighs 50 pounds, which is convenient for shipping. There are fewer broken boxes, and the loss of weight is not much. "Body" Most are baked dry and have enough moisture to prevent mold and worms and can be stored for a long time. "Goods" Sweeter, fresher, and more tender, with uniform particles. Even smaller particles are round, fleshy, and edible.

(Lanzhen Branches) "Packaging" Each box weighs about 100 jin. During shipping, the boxes are easily broken, and the weight loss is more significant. "Body" The baking process is often insufficient, and the water content is not exhausted, so it is easy to mold and worm. Sometimes, the heat is too strong, and the flesh turns black and tastes bitter. Both over and under are difficult to store for a long time and are not suitable. It is best to dry them in the sun, which makes the shell and flesh bright and lovely. However, when it is cloudy and rainy, baking is necessary, so attention must still be paid to the drying method. "Goods" The sweetness is less pronounced, and the undergrowth also has a slight sourness. If the flesh is not as tender as when it is freshly picked, the small nucleus and thick flesh can make up for its shortcomings. The particles are uneven, and the small particles are pointed, thin, and tasteless, merely a formality.

This year, the harvest of Lanzhu branches in Zhangzhou was normal, so the local prices were higher when the new goods were released, which was not very suitable for sales. Later, due to the influx of Jinshan branches, prices fell to compete with them. In addition, because there were too many pointed particles in the goods, sales were almost zero. Even now, not only has the selling price fallen behind that of Jinshan branches, but sales have also remained sluggish. The main reason is that the goods are impure. During periods of market , goods should be superior in order to gain a foothold. Otherwise, there will be no failure.

Food

Standard Flour Market Shows Slight Uptrend in Later Trading 211

丨Dalian Group's Spot Flour Liquidated Slightly丨

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, each month generally showed a stable trend. As the prices of foreign wheat only fluctuated by a few points, the market was generally flat at the beginning. However, each factory remained on the sidelines, and transactions were very quiet. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, transactions seemed to be slightly smoother, as the Dalian Group liquidated spot flour, and futures also showed a slight recovery. As for the factory situation, Fufeng bought near-term positions due to strong spot demand but sold off a large number of far-term positions. Fuxin sold near-term positions and left far-term positions unchanged. Therefore, although the market showed an uptrend, the rise was not significant. However, as the prices of spot flour in this port were too high, and the Tianjin Group had not yet settled on many Dingbian flours, it seemed that manufacturers had to change their attitudes in order to avoid future worries. As a result, this month was slightly better by 2.5 li compared to the previous day, January was better by 5 li, February was better by 1.25 fen, March was unchanged, April was better by 7.5 li, and May was better by 2.5 li.

Free Talk Short Story The Thief (1) Zhu Their stomachs were empty, rumbling loudly. As they walked along those roads brighter than daylight, they felt truly impatient. The reds, the greens, the bright, the shiny, so many things to eat and use, but they could only look, with no benefit. Walking like this, they felt only hatred. They chose to walk in the dimly lit areas under the electric lights, passing through several streets, turning and twisting, until they truly reached a very dark place. This road was paved with small stones, far less smooth than the asphalt roads they had walked on before. The electric lights were so sparse, and they didn't know what kind of houses these were. The doors were all tightly closed. There were also a few places where a flickering, dim lamp shone from the narrow entrances, vaguely illuminating the red or black characters of "×× Grand Hotel." There were also some signs for buildings and restaurants, hanging there, strangely greasy. The electric lights in the small grocery stores were quite bright on the wide street. From several dark alley entrances, there were stalls baking sesame cakes, two or three men with greasy faces sitting on long benches, like monkeys, one foot curled up, squatting on the edge of the bench, both hands tightly hugging their knees, their expressions as if they had been drowsing for half a day. "It looks like this place will do." "Okay, let's go a little further. We need to find a place where we can stretch our legs and arms. If there's no food, then fine, let's just sleep well and see what happens tomorrow!" They couldn't be blamed for feeling this way. These two weak sentences, scattered in the air, were so clear and chilling. Approaching the edge of a wider set of stone steps, Sanda pulled on the corner of Dafa's coat, and with a turn, Dafa fell to the ground. "Sanda, I'm telling you, this really is a good place." Sanda stretched his legs out very straight, feeling that all his joints were comfortable, letting Dafa's words scatter in the silence, without answering. He suddenly kicked Dafa's butt, and even Dafa lay down with his legs stretched straight. "Damn it, why did you kick me, you son of a bitch?" Dafa cursed Sanda. "To make you sleep more comfortably. Why are you bending your butt?" Dafa had no words, and turned over again. In a few minutes, the snoring of the two men sounded together. Dafa saw the tall chimneys, piles of factory buildings. A young worker was telling him many things, and his heart seemed to be pulled tightly by something, holding his breath, thinking in his heart. Just as he was holding his breath, he heard two very clear snapping sounds, which somehow drove the young worker away. He immediately opened his eyes, looking for clarity. Then he heard the sharp sound of a police whistle, and suddenly sat up, looking around at the dim street. All the factories and workers were just a dream. A shadow flashed before his eyes, and then several more snaps sounded in succession. He didn't understand what was going on. He pushed Sanda, who didn't wake up. Looking back, he saw two people standing at the entrance of a store, saying things he didn't understand. Dafa couldn't help but ask: "What's going on?" A middle-aged man turned his head, made an annoyed expression, and turned his head back. "Catching hobos, catching robbers!" Another younger man said to Dafa. He really wanted to see what catching robbers was like. Seeing someone running ahead, he followed and ran in that direction. After sleeping for a while, he didn't know where the strength came from. He caught up with that person and turned to the right. The street was even darker here. After running a short distance, he saw several men in coarse cloth clothes gathered together, looking ahead at a white, misty street. He lost his original interest and joined the group of people. He really didn't expect to see an injured person lying there, a large patch of bright red blood smeared on the dark road, half of his clothes soaked in blood. "This is truly making a wronged ghost. I don't know where those two robbers have escaped to," said a man with a full beard, gesturing wildly. Dafa finally understood. He looked again at the wronged ghost on the ground, a young man, but when he looked up at the other people, he couldn't find a single face that showed surprise or sympathy. "Oh, a scapegoat, a wronged ghost, a starving ghost, there are countless of them every day. We ourselves don't even know what kind of ghost we'll be tomorrow," the man said and left. "Hatred" and "Love" Xing "Hatred" and "love" are the source of life, which is to say, the vitality of life. Without "hatred" and "love," perhaps this universe would become a wasteland. For example, the Russian Revolution, which they claimed was based on "hatred." And the National Revolution led by Mr. Sun Yat-sen was based on "love," so Mr. Sun often wrote the two characters "universal love" when giving inscriptions. Can you deny the great power of "love" and "hatred"? The opposition of "love" and "hatred" is just like "laughter" and "crying," but without "love," there would be no "hatred," just as without "crying," there would be no "laughter." The "power of love" certainly makes people feel relaxed and comfortable, as if sitting in a spring breeze, but it can sometimes lead to relaxation. After relaxation, one will feel tired. And "hatred," if it cannot be vented, will be like a poisonous snake, forever gnawing at our hearts. For example, the "hatred of national subjugation" of Korea and India, will this hatred ever have an end? Furthermore, when Yang Guifei hanged herself, Bai Juyi also wrote a high poem "Song of Everlasting Regret" for her, and as for Daiyu's short life, there are still many "Baoyu" who hold regret for her for thousands of years, although it is said that this is only a private affair between children, unrelated to national affairs. "Hatred," "love," the source of life, the vitality of life, but what about our vitality of life? What about our source of life? Half of the Northeast territory has been cut away by others, and we are still indulging in decadent pleasures and singing and dancing in peace, is this "hatred"? Is it "love"? Or is it without hatred and without love? What is without hatred and without love? It is wood and stone, it is a pool of stagnant water. Let us stir up some waves in the stagnant water! Fundraising Ms. Wang Wanrong We were a group of eight people, dragged to Shizi Street near the school to raise military pay for the Northeast Volunteer Army. We had decided long ago: we would set off at eight in the morning and return for class at ten. "Is your master up yet? Please donate some military pay!" Mei said, when we walked into the first house. "Oh dear! Here they come again, asking for money! Get out quickly! If you wake up the old lady, she'll scold me again." A maid pushed Pei, Pei took a step back and stepped on my foot. I endured the pain and retreated with them! A chartered car was being pulled over from the east. Chun released her athletic nature, and started chasing after it. The driver couldn't outrun her. After only four or five steps, Chun grabbed him and said: "Please generously donate some military pay!" "Please donate four jiao, I'll give you a receipt, so if you encounter a fundraising team from another school later, you won't have to donate again." We also rushed over and surrounded the chartered car. Xue waved the receipt in her hand and said. "What military pay or no military pay? You female students go and fundraise from women! Do you even understand 'men and women should not touch hands'? How can you be chasing after men on the street?" No one expected that a young man wearing a suit with a badge on his chest would say such a thing. "This is terrible!" "How ridiculous!" "You traitorous bastard!" Everyone shouted. The driver broke through the encirclement and ran forward! We walked into the second house! What a big mansion! An old lady was supervising several servants making flour balls. "Please donate some military pay!" Rong put the bamboo donation container on the nearby table, saying this. She was really exhausted! "Girls! We never donate here. We are not from Suzhou," the old lady refused, saying. "That's right! Because you have never donated before, we must ask you to donate a little today. It doesn't matter whether you are from Suzhou or not, in any case, you are a Chinese citizen. If the Volunteer Army wasn't fighting the Japanese in the Northeast, would you still be able to eat flour balls?" I said. Really, who would believe her? Speaking in a completely pure Suzhou dialect, and still trying to deny it, what's the point of denying it? "Eating is something everyone has to do! How can anyone not eat?" The old lady glared at me. "Yes," I said again. "In order to make sure the Volunteer Army doesn't have to fight on an empty stomach, we came out to fundraise!" "Oh dear! I won't talk to you all anymore! You female students are so eloquent and speak so nicely! How can us old women win against you? Fine, take a few coppers! Do you want them or not?" The old woman threw three coppers onto the table. Ying picked them up and stuffed them into the bamboo container. "Actually, you are doing this with good intentions..." the old woman continued to babble. I couldn't help but laugh. We took her three coppers and stopped talking. Of course it was "good intentions"! We walked into the third house, into a large hall. Four or five accountants were calculating rent rice, striking the abacus beads crisply and skillfully! "Oh dear! Here come the fundraisers again! Let me be honest with you: we don't want to be fooled again!" A man with glasses said, looking at the characters on our banner. "Take ten coppers! You can buy a few big cakes to eat. There are plenty of silver dollars and banknotes, but..." A short, fat man spoke the most venomously! Who knows where he saw students buying big cakes with the money they raised? But no one argued with him. Arguing with an ignorant person is the most foolish thing to do. We finally accepted the money and retreated! After walking to over a hundred households, seeing enough ugly faces, and hearing enough unpleasant words, the coppers we raised hadn't even filled a third of our bamboo container. "Sigh, why are Chinese people so selfish?" Mei shook her head and sighed. "Sigh..." Pei also shook her head and took a breath of cold air. Cat Youming Mo Bo Sang said: "All poets love cats," I feel that this sentence is very reasonable; because of the gentle nature of cats, lively posture, smiling face, fine and soft fur, agile climbing ability, is really all lovable! Friends who like to play with cats, once they see this appearance, always can't help but shout: "This lively little thing, little guy, clever little darling". Not to mention sensitive poets! I am also a cat lover, but I don't have the talent of a poet and can't express my liking for cats, which is a pity. The ancients said: "Cats are reincarnated from seven generations of young women (prostitutes)." This probably refers to their frivolity and coquettishness. I have raised several cats, but halfway through, they either died or were lost, so the memories they left me are very deep. I remember when I was sixteen years old, I raised a cat, that cat left me with the deepest memories, I really loved that cat at that time! Although it was lost later, I still remember it: That cat was obtained from my aunt's house. At that time, it had only been out of its mother's belly for two months, but it was already running and jumping like a little tiger. I liked its smallness and liveliness, so I asked my aunt for it. It was considered the most lively and lovable one in the nest. The color of the kitten was very beautiful, a mixture of yellow, white, and black, like a lively and lovely little tiger, adding to its "tiger shape." However, it was not as big and fierce as a tiger. It was full of "vitality," with round eyes, fine and soft fur, gentle nature, lively posture, like a happy girl, full of brightness and purity. It was truly a typical cat! There was also that short, round body, growing fine and soft downy hair, a round and lovely little head, the most prominent two gypsum-like small ears, that round, pointed chin, and exquisite little mouth, so lovable! Ah! There was also that red little nose, slightly moist, shining with a watery light. That kitten had a unique innocence, always jumping around all day long, never stopping, and when it jumped, its nimble little body seemed very lively and interesting. One day, I came home from school, ate lunch, and basked in the sun in the hallway. I unintentionally saw the little calico cat sitting "refreshed" on the threshold. It had a very good "horse stance," sitting stably and upright. That kind of great spirit was like a hero commanding a million soldiers, and also like a big bug dominating in the deep mountains! At that time, I almost jumped up! I was very excited, a kind of desire gradually rose in my body, rose along my nerves, ran in my limbs, making my teeth clench, my hands had an unbearable itching, I quickly clenched my fists. That lively little thing/little guy was sitting there looking down on everything, sometimes turning its lively and alert little head, as if searching for something, sometimes using its soft forelimbs, the forelimbs with the sharp claws retracted, wiping its round, pointed face indifferently. I observed for a while, wanting to wait for it to finish wiping its face before grabbing it into my arms. But it just kept wiping its/light red little nose calmly. I got annoyed waiting, so I strode over and hugged the little guy tightly. Its trembling limbs and fine, soft fur slid in my hands, and I felt a kind of mysterious heat. This heat made me relax my hands, which were holding it tightly because I felt it was too cute. I embraced it very gently, caressed it very lovingly, and combed its fur. It was very happy, murmuring softly, rolling in my arms, its lovely forelimbs, which had retracted their sharp claws, waving wildly in the air, like small hands wanting to fold something. I turned it over, and the sunlight stimulated its eyelids, making it feel very uneasy, it narrowed its eyelids and screamed "Meow! Meow!" in anger. I knew it was annoyed, so I turned it over again and put it on the ground. It jumped down, feeling very free, stretched its waist, stood up, shook its body a few times, and ran away very lively with a "Tuk!······Tuk!" A few days later, I unintentionally walked into the dining room and saw it arching its back, standing up its tail,贴on the corner of the wall, I was curious and went closer to observe. It turned out that A Wang (dog's name) was picking up bone shells under the dining table to eat. For its safety, I held it in my arms, its limbs were still shaking slightly, at this time it was lying in my arms very comfortably and coquettishly, two emerald green eyes looking at me with a glimmering radiance. I chased A Wang away and then let it down. I took a rope and teased it with it, and it held up its cute little forelimbs like small hands and chased after it. A Wang thought we were gone and came back silently with his head lowered. I chased him away again, and he was startled. I felt he was too rude and barbaric, like the fellow in "Water Margin" Flower Monk from Mount Wutai, because he had repeatedly stolen the chicken feed, so I hated him very much. Although A Wang was chased away by me, he ran a few steps and suddenly turned around and looked at us fiercely and unkindly, looking jealous. His ears were standing straight up, and a pair of round eyes were emitting a wolf-like green light. He thought, "Why are you protecting this little thing/little guy so well? This little thing/bad kid is so naughty, running and jumping so happily in front of the little master, climbing lively, with a smiling face, and acting coquettishly with the little master, and also struggling in the cage. This kind of frivolous behavior, naturally can't get into his eyes, so he could only say 'Qiang' and run elsewhere with his head lowered, 'lost'." One afternoon, I came home from school and suddenly felt lonely. I wanted to play with the kitten, but I looked everywhere and couldn't find a trace of the lovely kitten; at that time, I felt a wisp of inexplicable sadness in my heart. Could it be that the little thing that had been with me for the past few months was lost? Or was it that someone saw how cute it was and took it away? At that time, I felt very melancholy. Day after day passed, and when I had free time after school, I always felt lost and unhappy. After a while, I heard a neighbor say: "Your family's kitten was taken away by a strange passerby one afternoon." At that time, I received confirmation. I have raised several cats, and the feelings it left me are the deepest, so I always have good feelings for cats. Cats are indeed a lovely little animal/a loyal domestic animal. Amateur Weekly (Hengzhi) Second Issue Amateur Ramblings Hints of Awakening Dawn of Transformation Pu Since the launch of the first issue of Amateur Weekly and the employee communication column met with readers, what inspires the reporter most is more than two hundred letters discussing the issues and manuscripts describing the various tragic and inhuman lives of workers and apprentices. On the employee side, although they are in a higher position than workers and apprentices, in reality, the economic pressure and the suffering of intellectual hunger are not much different. We analyze the content of the letters and submissions we have received, and almost 90% of them are about economic difficulties and extremely hard work, as well as issues of how to continue to improve knowledge in their spare time. At this time when internal strife has not stopped and diplomacy is most urgent, the reporter listened to these many sincere, angry, and hell-like cries of resentment, and could not help but feel extremely sad. We see this Europeanized Shanghai, on one side it is so magnificent and splendid, and on the other side it is so gloomy and cruel. The future of the country has really reached an unimaginable point. However, in a flash, I thought that these cries contain infinite hints of awakening and a glimmer of transformation. If we can materialize this ability to awaken and amplify this glimmer of transformation, it may not be an insider's path to saving the nation and ourselves, so I unconsciously became excited again. However, how can we achieve this method of materialization and amplification is a creative problem that belongs to the realm of not having a teacher to inherit. We who grew up in this fragmented society are of course without any experience to speak of. Therefore, we now only have the attitude of researching and experimenting at the same time, and explore step by step. We only need to firmly believe that the transformation of the small environment is created by a few people, and the transformation of the big environment is created by the majority of people. We believe that the more we research and experiment, the more we can increase the formation of materialization and amplify the possibility of transformation. Speaking of this, I may as well take a suggestion from a letter that the reporter just received from Hong Jun to end this rambling, and at the same time give everyone an inspiration for research. The general idea of Hong Jun's letter is that most of the oppression of the environment suffered by most apprentices is the same. Most of them live a life of unhappiness all day long. Therefore, Hong Jun suggested that all the apprentices who read this journal should take this opportunity to have the journal act as an intermediary, and then each person should communicate with each other, and mutually express their opinions on improving their living environment. If this allows people with similar personalities to gradually become familiar with each other, and then further become intimate friends, wouldn't it be of great benefit in terms of improving life and cultivating scholarship? The reporter deeply feels that Hong Jun's suggestion has great research value, and specifically proposes it here as a reference for everyone's awakening and transformation. As for the original text of the letter, it will be announced in the employee communication column on another day, and readers are welcome to express their opinions. Issue Discussion Problem of Improving Amateur Entertainment Amateur Entertainment and Playing Mahjong Yeping Anyone can believe that almost most of the amateur enthusiasts are spending their precious and limited entertainment time on playing mahjong. Because of this widespread fact, especially in Shanghai or other larger cities, playing mahjong is an open gambling behavior, so it has value worth discussing and researching. Our starting point for discussion is: amateur entertainment is absolutely necessary. Because after a person has gone through more than eight hours of office life every day, they are mentally extremely tired or depressed. Although sleep can restore the spirit, if there are only two monotonous and cyclical lifestyles of sleep and work every day, that is absolutely impossible. That will simply shorten your life geometrically. This is something that must be paid attention to in life. Secondly, we want to discuss whether playing mahjong is suitable for amateur entertainment? I can say with certainty that playing mahjong is absolutely not suitable for amateur entertainment. Besides the harm, you can't find any benefits from it. Over time, after you get used to playing, first, you will inevitably suffer losses materially. In total, none of the people who play mahjong can win money, otherwise, there will be no money for the first game. The four people playing mahjong and the owner are like five tanks, one empty in the middle, like the owner, and four around are filled with water, like the four people playing mahjong. So the process of winning or losing in each game of mahjong is like scooping water from the four tanks with water and scooping it back and forth, and each time you scoop, you must drop some into the empty tank, which is what is called "playing the first game". After continuing like this for a long time, the result is: the four tanks that were originally filled with water are almost exhausted, and the empty tank that had no water originally, the empty tank that reaps the benefits, does the opposite and gets a full tank of water. Therefore, the four people sitting and playing mahjong, statistically speaking day by day, none of them do not lose money, but the degree of loss is somewhat different. Under the current social situation, money is an element of life, and since money is lost, it will definitely be related to mental pain. But there is even worse. If you don't play mahjong, it's fine, but once you start playing mahjong, you play four rounds--at least four rounds, then another four rounds, and then another four rounds, ..., you won't stop until everyone is exhausted and can't sit anymore! This is a common problem. Therefore, once you start, you often have to stay up until two or three in the morning before you can sleep, or even fight all night long! In this way, no matter how strong your body is, as a result, gradually, at first, your body feels a little uncomfortable, headache, back pain, ..., and later, inevitably, neurasthenia, insomnia, and other similar diseases will climb onto your body. Friends, may I ask what is the original intention of entertainment? The above is just two of its most obvious harms. In addition, a person who likes to play mahjong will definitely not pay attention to hygiene. After playing cards, wiping their face, they immediately go to the office, which is a common occurrence. Even after finishing work the next day, they come back to do what they call the unfinished work from the day before. This is only harmful and not beneficial to the body, which can be asserted. In short, I sincerely hope that friends who play mahjong can jump out of this deep pit and embark on other proper paths. The Problem of Small Office Workers' Life Forced Transactions Hui Zheng "Gift-giving" is something that often troubles us small office workers in the company. After the general affairs department sends the salary every month, it is often found that there are always a few yuan less, sometimes even a third of it is deducted, the reason is; the general affairs department sent a few gifts on your behalf and deducted the money. The income of senior staff is much higher than ours. Of course, deducting a few yuan from them is not a big deal. (There is still important text, turn to the second page)

Page 22

However, for us small office workers with thirty or forty yuan, it is a bit of a problem. Originally, apart from the necessary living expenses, there is not a penny left. In this way, we have no choice but to go into debt. Therefore, we all sigh in unison about "gift-giving". Originally, "gift-giving" was based on the feelings between humans. A has something worth commemorating or happy, such as having a child, and people who have good feelings with A will send him a gift, on the one hand to increase his happiness, on the other hand to leave him a souvenir. Again, if A encounters a sad or unfortunate event, such as the death of his parents, he will also send a gift to comfort his soul, but in modern times, especially in Shanghai, it has become a kind of "forced transaction". Not to mention friends with feelings, even a colleague among thousands of people who has nothing to do with me must also send a gift, and sometimes, I don't even know what the face of the gift recipient looks like. When you have something going on, I have to send a gift and have a meal. When I have something going on, you also have to send a gift and come for a meal. Formally speaking, it is "gift-giving", but in essence, it is a "forced transaction". (Those who borrow things to extort money are another matter) Again, speaking from the whole of society, this is an infinitely large waste! The national crisis is getting deeper and deeper, and the country is getting poorer and poorer. Let's slow down and talk about "frugality" to save the country. Why don't we first eliminate this infinitely large waste in society - gift-giving? A little less waste, of course, saves us from a bit of poverty, which also saves the country a bit of wealth. Eliminate the habit of "gift-giving", and at the same time, do not accept other people's gifts, and organize a non-gift-giving alliance. I think this is precisely the seed of our amateur social movement in the industrial and commercial world! Rice Market Reaches Peak Season, Then Declines 215

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, over fifty boats arrived, but sales in this street were not good. The opening prices of various goods had limited fluctuations. Sales of Changshu-Wuxi North Non-glutinous rice felt sluggish, while high-priced rice was weak. The Shanghai-Tongxiang variety held steady. The overall market only saw minor activity from rural residents and small merchants. There is still a large inventory of early and late rice. Out-of-town merchants were interested in inquiring about higher-quality rice, and the situation was stable. The price of Yinyuan rice remained unchanged. The "Shuailuo" (a brand) was selling at three "chi".

(New Zhabei) Yesterday, over thirty boats arrived from various regions, but market sales slumped. Trading of North Non-glutinous rice was not active, and the market was flat. The price of foreign Dujian rice had been rising sharply for several days. However, because arrivals were scarce, the price decreased slightly. The sales of early and late rice were average. Similar to the thick Non-glutinous rice, the trend was stable. The sales of "Bianyuan" brand products were sluggish, and arrivals were not abundant, presenting a steady situation.

Foreign Rice Sales Stagnant, Prices Decline 216

Lower Small Rice by Two Cents; Foreign Rice Weakens by Five Cents

Yesterday, the market conditions for foreign rice continued to be weak. As the supply of foreign rice continued to arrive, sales remained sluggish, and inventories gradually increased. Recently, the Southern merchant group is adopting a wait-and-see attitude, due to the impending implementation of river rice circulation. The Northern merchant group has completely halted operations. From now on, they will only pay attention to river Non-glutinous rice. This street no longer has any interest, and the market price immediately started to fall. Sellers are also willing to lower prices to sell off their inventory. Customers have begun to inquire due to the lower prices. In the general market, 320 bags of Hunan machine-milled red rice from Fuzhou and Quanzhou were sold at a price of 7.9 yuan, and 200 bags of machine-milled oil rice were sold at a price of 8.75 to 8.78 yuan, both slightly higher than the previous day by more than five cents. This street sold 150 bags of Xiaojiao rice at a price of 7.6 yuan, which was two cents lower.

Silk and Tea

Wuxi Stores Silk Cocoons, Transports to Shanghai for Sales 217

Recently, the silk market in foreign firms has continued to decline. The economic recession in Europe and the United States, coupled with the encroachment of Japanese silk and artificial silk, has led to a slump in Chinese silk sales. Telegrams from white silk factories all complain about the high prices and refuse to buy. Silk merchants have been accumulating silk stocks and lack the funds to turn over. The situation is difficult to maintain. Wuxi is the central area for silk cocoons. There are a total of 50 silk factories in the county. After the new cocoons were launched this year, more than 20 factories started production. Due to the increasingly sluggish silk sales, closures have followed. Currently, only 13 factories are barely operating. Dried cocoons are not being inquired about. As the end of the year approaches, cocoon merchants are transporting stored cocoons to Shanghai for sale. As a result, nearly 4,000 "dan" of cocoons have been transported to Shanghai in the past month.

Luzhuang’s "Zhenmei" Tea Sells Smoothly to France 218

Yesterday, "Zhenmei" recorded tea from Luzhuang, English firms, and Jinlong, Tongfu, Baochang and Yishi (洋行名) Foreign Firms all started trading activiely with brisk transactions and a stable market. Needle tea and pearl tea also had scattered sales. The green tea market has a momentum for gradual movement, but Qining black tea, English and Russian merchants are taking a wait-and-see approach, and sales are stagnant.

Oil Market

Hankou Asphalt Continues to Drop in Price 219

Since asphalt prices fell in Hankou, sales in this port remain sluggish. However, the Zhejiang region, conversely, is experiencing a supply shortage. Market conditions are moving in opposite directions to those of Hankou. This is due to differing conditions across regions. According to telegrams from Hankou, market prices have fallen further. According to Chongjing, the opening price was 12 taels. Tianjin City's price was only 11 taels. Prices are falling rapidly, and the situation is like a burst dam. However, Zhejiang oil remains strong. The phenomenon of prices rising in the south while falling in the north goes against common sense. However, Zhejiang oil only affects a small area, unlike the broad coverage of the Hankou market. Furthermore, the market in this port usually follows Hankou's lead. Therefore, even if Zhejiang oil has momentum, it will not be affected, and the selling price will still fall according to Hankou's market. This may stimulate sales and allow circulation into Zhejiang Province.

White Tung Oil Gradually Stabilizes 220

Since the price of white tung oil at Hankou Foreign Firms reached 17.78 taels, transactions have been intermittent and unpredictable. According to details from yesterday's Hankou letter, there is a significant supply, leading to a weak market. Traders are selling for only 13.4 taels in foreign silver. Local firms previously bought a batch of futures from Hangzhou traders, ranging from 23.34 yuan to 22.67 yuan per "shi". Now, due to the decline in the Hankou market, although Zhejiang Province can still maintain its position, the enthusiasm of buyers is not as strong as before. Therefore, they have gradually adopted a wait-and-see attitude recently. However, according to various producing areas, sellers are unwilling to sell at too low prices due to cost considerations. As a result, Zhejiang tung oil seems to be in a stable state. Although Hankou prices have fallen, sales have not been stimulated. Further price drops are unlikely, and the time for a turnaround has not yet arrived. A period of stability can still be expected.
